
-----title

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年</a>　为表兄李叔翔跋马遵所传《七君子帖》后。作品：《七君子帖》、《跋家藏七君子帖》<div id='poem_1317938' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317938' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317938?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋家藏七君子帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1252年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317938")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317938_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317938'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317938'>七君子帖，其一为杨文公，其二为文潞公，其三为张文定公，其四为欧阳公，其五为东坡公，其六为韩魏公，其七未详，末有题辞，则梁溪尤延之先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317938_comment'></div>尤公，乾、淳名儒，其子木石先生端明公煜，宝祐间提纲史事，以校勘辟余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317938_comment'></div>是数帖者，虽纸敝墨渝，不可尽读，而三百馀年典刑文献在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317938_comment'></div>《诗》云「云谁之思？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317938_comment'></div>西方美人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317938_comment'></div>彼美人兮，西方之人兮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317938_comment'></div>谨书以贻子孙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1317938_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年8月</a>　八月，丁母忧，家居守孝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年</a>　居母丧在家。作品：《祭咸宁郡太夫人文》<div id='poem_1318010' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318010' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318010?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭咸宁郡太夫人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1266年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1318010")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318010_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318010'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318010'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318010_comment'></div>诸孤失母，亦既踰年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318010_comment'></div>母棺在堂，如闻其声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318010_comment'></div>母像在几，如见其容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318010_comment'></div>孰知日月有期，体魄则降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318010_comment'></div>母之声容，将去此而何之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318010_comment'></div>年开八帙，而半世嫠居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318010_comment'></div>禄集暮龄，而一生淡泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318010_comment'></div>藐是诸孤，其何以报吾母乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318010_comment'></div>畴昔京师，戏䌽成图，母谓诸孙，吾不复此乐矣，异时见我，其徵诸画工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318010_comment'></div>孰知此语之竟为不祥乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318010_comment'></div>浙江潮平，理棹将发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318010_comment'></div>呼母而别，泪涕长潸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318010_comment'></div>孰知此生之不可再见乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318010_comment'></div>金鹅之阡，相其阴阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318010_comment'></div>慈母之德，孝娥相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318010_comment'></div>山联丑艮，面直未坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318010_comment'></div>以妥尊灵，以庇来云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318010_comment'></div>穆卜良辰，輀车既启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318010_comment'></div>血泪彻泉，终天而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318010_comment'></div>呜呼痛哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1318010_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年11月</a>　十一月，葬亡母段氏于金鹅塘（在乐平谭水滨）<br /></div><div class='label1' id='23d8411f39924d59ac88660cef3e2dcf_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1289')">1275-1289年</a>，54-68岁</div><div id='23d8411f39924d59ac88660cef3e2dcf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　廷鸾自号玩芳病叟。参知政事陈文龙致诗，和之。作品：《陈菊圃参政寄诗千里外，托兴于秋燕春花，以示玩芳病叟。叟病，不能吟，强和四章。前二章借来意以自伤；后二章述愚怀以志感》<span class='inlineComment2'>（本年九月，陈文龙知兴化军，固守，元兵不能下。十二月，因通判开城降，文龙被执，不屈绝食而死。）</span><div id='poem_56642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_56642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56642'>斜阳对语归飞处，底是乌衣王谢家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56642_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56643?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_56643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56643'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56643'>桃李盘中天地宽，误渠鼎实为才悭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56643'>苔荒草没浑无耻，犹自青黄烟雨间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_56641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56641'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56641'>冠峨獬豸服绯花，欲献甘芹谓苦茶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56641'>误尽灵乌报凶吉，终然爰止托谁家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56641'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56641_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56640' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_56640_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56640'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56640'>灿灿黄花老圃宽，秋芳不采岂云悭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56640'>江南九日闽千里，尚挹寒香纸墨间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56640'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56640_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　宋亡，端临以父疾为由，不复出仕，隐居教授，远近师之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　廷鸾整理《子才集》，作跋。作品：《题院判学士家集后》、书御史龙图公集后。<div id='poem_1317922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题察判学士家集后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317922")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317922'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317922'>先世《子才集》十一卷，缮写藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317922_comment'></div>子才以诗文豪于熙宁、元祐间，迨淳熙中，矸轩程公为之谱其年，第其卷，订其述作大槩，而惜其器业之未底于成，于斯文用力多，寄意厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317922_comment'></div>去淳熙八十有七年，五世诸孙某，读遗编，抚而叹曰：程公谓子才元祐奏篇，论北事效于靖康，信然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317922_comment'></div>抑又诸史论，如论晋人以父母之邦委之于群胡，残暴戮辱，百馀年间，无有奋发以生吾中国之气，又安得有奇士哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317922_comment'></div>如论后魏，谓中国以礼义文采之腴，而饲禽兽之饥，此之谓不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317922_comment'></div>非吾一人之可与之争，吾必激天下之气，而与魏争，古之善战者，能用天下之气而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317922_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317922_comment'></div>安得此语闻于炎、绍中兴之初乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317922_comment'></div>子才从节孝徐先生游且久，其文章雄直，雅似节孝，今取《徐集》三诗系《家集》后，而著其说如此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1317922_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317921' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317921' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317921?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书御史龙图公集后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317921")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317921_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317921'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317921'>龙图先公《文集》十卷，某缮写家藏，点校既毕，抚而叹曰：公所谓谏书，知无不言，言无不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317921_comment'></div>然每篇不过数百字，有他人谆复千言所不到者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317921_comment'></div>《论命相疏》，举崔群《开元天宝理乱》之说而申之，曰：「譬犹养身，常须慎病，不可以觉痛之日，始为受病之辰」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317921_comment'></div>至哉言乎，又崔群所未发者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317921_comment'></div>《初劾宰相疏》，简严特甚，争之不胜，而犹有拳拳惜国体，不敢尽言之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317921_comment'></div>后世台谏劾大吏，掎摭怒骂，不遗馀力者，可少愧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317921_comment'></div>诗词流丽有风致，昔王荆公谓公「始读书，即以文词辩丽天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317921_comment'></div>赵忠定镇成都，奉诏编本朝《名臣奏议》，蜀之钜公李季章兄弟，实与论次，于公奏篇，录之无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317921_comment'></div>国史称公：「善议论，其言时政，不为激讦，故多见推行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317921_comment'></div>此数言者，足以尽公矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317921_comment'></div>不肖裔孙，何足以知之，书示后人云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1317921_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>　廷鸾为长男端复求婚庐山谢氏。作品：《庐山谢氏求婚启》<div id='poem_1317889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317889?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山谢氏求婚启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1277年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317889")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317889_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317889'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317889'>人于同年，已缔两家之好；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317889_comment'></div>吾求妇氏，将寻八载之盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317889_comment'></div>昔期开监宅之屏，今重感山阳之笛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317889_comment'></div>风雨如晦，俾无尤兮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317889_comment'></div>凤凰于飞，是有庆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317889_comment'></div>风帆匪远，星户有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317889_comment'></div>季秋于是御轮，仲夏为之将篚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317889_comment'></div>亲交币帛，无迟《归妹》之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317889_comment'></div>儿大诗书，是叶《家人》之吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317889_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1317889_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>　秋，作祭母诗。作品：《秋谒屺瞻诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（屺瞻，廷鸾母墓名。）</span><div id='poem_56825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋谒屺瞻墓</a><span class='authorDate'>（1277年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56825")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56825'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56825'>了知五十六年非，何处空山叫阿㜷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56825'>斗酒只鸡双泪落，荒林宿莽九原悲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56825'>黄花委地伤徂岁，青笋迎船忆旧时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56825'>庐下夜来霜屦冷，袜材持送懒残师。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56825'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56825_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>　山中，对紫薇花有感，怀故国，作诗。作品：《山中对紫薇花书感》<div id='poem_56707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山中对紫薇花书感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1277年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56707")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56707'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56707'>轻盈插向胆瓶中，看到山林禁籞同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56707'>阁下天葩秋月黯，楼头奎画晓云空<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56707'>高攀玉树扶斑白<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，静扫苍苔拾堕红<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56707'>三十年前天上梦，老来无泪洒西风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56707'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_56707'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_56707_0'>⑴ 自注：紫薇阁三大金字乃宁宗御书。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_56707_0'>⑵ 自注：太府寺一株独盛，余尝侍亲其下。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_56707_0'>⑶ 自注：西省五株苔痕满砌，余尝草制其中。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_56707_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年</a>　元世祖招马廷鸾赴阙，不至。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年</a>　著《洙泗裔编》并书后。作品：《书洙泗裔编后》<div id='poem_1317926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书洙泗裔编后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1278年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317926")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317926'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317926'>《论语》、《家语》、《孔丛子》，皆孔氏家书也，而有粹驳之不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317926_comment'></div>《家语》驳于《论语》，《孔丛子》又驳于《家语》，盖更春秋而战国，战国而秦汉，孔氏之家学，其亦与世道相为升降也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317926_comment'></div>《家语》自安国撰次，当孝成时，其孙愆上书自言，而不得立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317926_comment'></div>至魏王肃，始得之孔子二十二世孙猛，而后传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317926_comment'></div>《孔丛子》至本朝宋咸，始著明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317926_comment'></div>其书朱文公诋其鄙浅，不列诸子之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317926_comment'></div>岁在戊寅，某读书山中，感时抚事，悼斯文兴丧之不可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317926_comment'></div>适架上抽取《孔丛子》书读之，因摘雅正不缪于圣人者，抄为此编，且附所见于逐段之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317926_comment'></div>因窃自叹于吾夫子，受罔极之恩，则夫诵其诗，读其书，可不尚论其世乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317926_comment'></div>乃并考沂水侯以降出处世次之本末，遂为之说，曰：呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317926_comment'></div>世变之推移，可畏哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317926_comment'></div>自春秋、战国以逮秦、汉，先圣子孙，阅历多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317926_comment'></div>鲋为陈涉博士，而子建不肯仕莽朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317926_comment'></div>霸辞三公，而光附王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317926_comment'></div>当世道将更，与其革命之际，其于为人，贤不肖何如也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317926_comment'></div>其处平世，则僖之坚刚，季彦之直清，亦可以见其先人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317926_comment'></div>东汉以后迄有唐，徒闻封爵之号，而其人不少槩见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317926_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317926_comment'></div>世变之推移，可畏哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1317926_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　题徐霖赠诗后。作品：《题徐径畈赠诗帖后》<div id='poem_1317943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题徐径畈赠诗帖后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317943")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317943'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317943'>故殿讲右司徐公，名霖，字景说，衢人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317943_comment'></div>去城二十里，所居名径畈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317943_comment'></div>初为举子时，师事乡先生晦静汤公，晦静以英才目之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317943_comment'></div>为甲辰礼部进士第一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317943_comment'></div>史嵩之之为相也，专权固位，植党欺君，弃贤任佞，公论切齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317943_comment'></div>徐公以新进士，一日叩阍上书，白发其奸，海内惊叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317943_comment'></div>亡何，嵩之败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317943_comment'></div>明年乙巳，朝廷更化，穆陵思其忠，自待次教官，给札入馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317943_comment'></div>丙午在馆，丁未参详省试院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317943_comment'></div>余时以举人入试，所为文，知举监试稍见推许，议置前列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317943_comment'></div>诸公所拟殊未定，徐公独指余文，赞其决，遂叨首选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317943_comment'></div>待试亲策，亟访谢之，一见如平生欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317943_comment'></div>居京师，时时往来，则为余赋《碧梧精舍》古句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317943_comment'></div>会京师大旱，徐公以馆职言事，攻谏长、京尹，乞祠，不待命去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317943_comment'></div>穆陵至以亲笔命宰执谕留，不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317943_comment'></div>余亦成进士归，访之径畈山中，复为赋后三数篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317943_comment'></div>其《寒夜》章尾句云：「一飞一鸣动千岁，青灯相语鬓成丝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317943_comment'></div>今已为脱简，不可读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317943_comment'></div>辄以所记忆补之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317943_comment'></div>徐公材高气劲，道胜名立，四方之士望如景星凤皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317943_comment'></div>一时钜公元夫，或拟伦稍过，声闻响臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317943_comment'></div>而余独忧之，尝寓书，举古人所谓「末俗易高，险涂难尽」之语，薄奉规切焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317943_comment'></div>岁壬子，徐公再还朝，影附滋众，遂与同朝诸公交关而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317943_comment'></div>流落十年，壬戌之春，起家，守临汀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317943_comment'></div>徐公亦且收膏反液，期于用世，而天不假年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317943_comment'></div>余之得其手笔，距今三十有三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317943_comment'></div>天荒地老，纸敝墨渝，叙而藏之，示我后嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317943_comment'></div>今世岂复有斯人哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　许表兄赠诗，次韵。作品：《次许表兄后》<div id='poem_56724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56724' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56724?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次许表兄韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56724")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56724_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56724'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56724'>物换星移一慨然，天荒地老断鳌前。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56724'>岂无志士王官谷，亦有飞仙太华巅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56724'>我若加三逢本命，君今过一渐稀年。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56724'>两人中表俱头白，蜀馈才堪几幅笺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56724_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56724'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56724_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　廷鸾作启为次男端临求婚于昌江李氏。作品：《昌江李氏求婚启》、《求聘启》<div id='poem_1317891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昌江李氏求婚启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317891")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317891'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317891'>鹦鹉洲边，结言有夙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317891_comment'></div>枌榆社里，纳币自今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317891_comment'></div>婚姻孔云，风涛如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317891_comment'></div>生男已当户，相从园绮之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317891_comment'></div>娶妇先及邻，遐想朱陈之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317891_comment'></div>为之有室，得以及时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317891_comment'></div>樽酒缠红，订八月乘槎之约；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317891_comment'></div>幅书传素，念三星束楚之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317891_comment'></div>绵蕝陈仪，丝萝永好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317891_comment'></div>屏开金雀，行依监宅之门阑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317891_comment'></div>堂设绛纱，归诵家庭之经传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317891_comment'></div>益培远业，用副深期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317891_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1317891_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　又作启为三男端履求婚于吴园张氏。作品：《吴园张氏求聘启》<div id='poem_1317892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴园张氏求聘启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317892")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317892'>婚姻三纪，未乾秦晋之盟书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317892_comment'></div>嫁娶一村，宜入朱陈之图画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317892_comment'></div>兹吾偶也，矧我甥兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317892_comment'></div>伏承令爱，姆训源流，夙同家姓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317892_comment'></div>而某三男，父书梗概，期绍儒猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317892_comment'></div>问我诸姑，子婿犹子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317892_comment'></div>以承先祖，孙妇外孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317892_comment'></div>凤凰占世世之荣昌，羔雁缔亲亲之永好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317892_comment'></div>兰阶方茁，勉寻安邑第之宗风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317892_comment'></div>燕厦新成，早并表贤堂之英矩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1317892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　又作启为四男端蒙求婚于於越许氏。作品：《於越许氏求婚启》<div id='poem_1317894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>于越许氏求婚启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317894")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317894_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317894'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317894'>甥舅匪他，有亲则久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317894_comment'></div>男女以正，非币不交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317894_comment'></div>奠雁诹期，令龟协吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317894_comment'></div>四月惟夏，兹逢假大之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317894_comment'></div>三星在天，际彼绸缪之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317894_comment'></div>多惭聘玉，聊奉缠红。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317894_comment'></div>无乃太简乎？得以及时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317894_comment'></div>春雨自培于百草，仆宁无舐犊之怀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317894_comment'></div>夜膏勤诵于六经，公则有乘龙之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317894_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1317894_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　友人、姻婭费伯恭，因丧乱自闽而来，廷鸾挽之同处，唱酬甚多。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>　与长男端复，附注疏于《仪礼》正经之下，作序。作品：《仪礼本经注疏会编后序》<div id='poem_1317902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>仪礼本经注疏会编后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317902")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317902'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317902'>余生五十八年，未尝读《仪礼》之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317902_comment'></div>一日从败帙中得景德中官本《仪礼疏》，四帙，正经、注语皆标起止，而疏文列其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317902_comment'></div>盖古有明经、学究专科，《仪礼》经注，学者童而习之，不待屑屑然登载本文而已熟，其诵数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317902_comment'></div>王介甫新经既出，士不读书，如余之于《仪礼》者，皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317902_comment'></div>然不敢付之茫昧幽冥，将寻访本书传抄，庶几创通大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317902_comment'></div>然余老矣，惧其费日力，而迄无所补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317902_comment'></div>长儿请曰：「家有监本《仪礼》经注，可取而附益之以便观览」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317902_comment'></div>意欣然，命之整辑，釐为九帙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317902_comment'></div>手自点校，并取朱氏礼书，与其门人高弟黄氏、杨氏诸家续补之编，分章析条，题要其上，遂为完书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317902_comment'></div>抚而叹曰：兹所谓《仪礼》者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317902_comment'></div>韩昌黎之云岂欺我哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317902_comment'></div>其为书也，于奇辞奥旨中，有精义妙道焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317902_comment'></div>于纤悉委曲中，有明辨等级焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317902_comment'></div>不独欲人之善其生，且欲人之善其死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317902_comment'></div>不惟致严于冠婚、朝聘、乡射，而尤严于丧祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317902_comment'></div>后世徒以推士礼而达于天子，以为残阙不可考之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317902_comment'></div>徐而观之，一士也，天子之士与诸侯之士不同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317902_comment'></div>一大夫也，下大夫与上大夫不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317902_comment'></div>等而上之，固有可得而推者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317902_comment'></div>周公之经，何制之备也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317902_comment'></div>子夏之传，何文之奇也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317902_comment'></div>康成之注、公彦之疏，何学之博也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317902_comment'></div>小子识之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1317902_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>　居乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年</a>　拜母墓，作诗。作品：《拜屺瞻墓有感》<div id='poem_56742' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56742' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56742?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拜屺瞻墓有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56742")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56742_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56742'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56742'>我走金塘十五年，新年六十意凄然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56742'>扶藜策蹇趋庐下，洗盏将雏拜影前。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56742'>蠹化不妨松饮露，凤栖犹拟柏参天。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56742'>微吟缓步沧江晚，一抹青山落照边。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56742'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56742_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年10月8日</a>　作诗。作品：德寿宫古松，太上爱之，尝持御香酾酒祠土神，以祈屏蟊贼云。时绍兴壬午，思陵馘亮之岁也。于今百二十年矣。仆生六十年后，而十月八日，又思陵上仙之晨，感而有赋。<div id='poem_56783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>德寿宫古松太上爱之尝持御香酾酒祠土神以祈屏蟊贼云时绍兴壬午思陵馘亮之岁也于今百二十年矣仆生六十年后而十月八日又思陵上仙之晨感而有赋<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年10月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56783")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56783'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56783'>六龙亲御奠神州，甲子如今甫再周。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56783'>百世尚瞻虞帝祀，五传遽抱杞天忧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56783'>臣民莫废瓜华敬，今古长悲禾黍秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56783'>叹息馀生孤露甚，门弧弓棘总成愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56783_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56783'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56783_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56782?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年10月8日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56782'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56782'>南来天马总辛勤，内禅经今历再壬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56782'>复汉赤符还旧宇，法尧黄屋本非心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56782'>思成门外衣冠尽，德寿宫前茨棘深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56782'>叹息馀生孤露甚，匪莪彼黍涕淋淫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56782_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56782'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56782_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年</a>　生日，张龙山致寿词，次其韵。作品：《齐天乐·和张龙山寿词》<div id='poem_56845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>齐天乐 和张龙山寿词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56845")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56845'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56845'>老夫耄矣，怪新年顿尔，□衰俱现。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56845'>排闷篇诗，浇愁盏酒，自读离骚自劝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56845'>长安日远。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56845'>怅旧国禾宫，故侯瓜畹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56845'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_56845", 56845, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>风景不殊</span>，江涛如此世缘浅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56845_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56845'>莫莫休休□□，□□乾坤毁，幽怀无限。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56845'>弱羽填波，轻装浮海，其奈沧溟潋滟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56845'>年华婉娩。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56845'>况六十平头，底须顽健。<div id='poem_sentence_8_56845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_56845'>戏唱高词，作还丹九转。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_56845_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　四月，成《读庄笔记》，作序，钩玄撮要，以寄“感时忧道”之志。<div id='poem_1317898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读庄笔记序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317898")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317898_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317898'>余读《庄子》，三十二年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317898_comment'></div>注家谓暂时揽其馀芳，犹足旷然有忘形自得之怀，况三十二年之久乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317898_comment'></div>虽然，一掩卷而茫然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317898_comment'></div>间尝先后得林竹溪、吕吉甫之《全解》，汤东涧之《略说》，唐成玄英之《义疏》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317898_comment'></div>有武林褚道士者，荟萃诸家之说，迄内外篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317898_comment'></div>林参以禅家，固其所自悟者，而又每每欲以文字关键论，则恐不满南华一笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317898_comment'></div>只令庄、老为一宗，自能成章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317898_comment'></div>然其胸中鳞甲，正与《晋史》所称郭象一辈人物相近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317898_comment'></div>汤公意象高远，时一著语，不规规于成书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317898_comment'></div>若成、褚两家，皆是浮屠、老子之绪言耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317898_comment'></div>成特为浅近，褚之所抄，差足以尽众说，其用功亦勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317898_comment'></div>余取诸书，手抄以附郭注，而自览焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317898_comment'></div>尝窃以为庄子，战国人也，去圣人之世若此其未远也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317898_comment'></div>又蒙人也，近圣人之居则又若此其未遥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317898_comment'></div>彼既不肯北学于中国，又未尝与知言养气之君子上下其议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317898_comment'></div>故其为说，凌高厉空，于吾圣人之书，曾未数数然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317898_comment'></div>后之解者，欲一二以圣人之书律之，则舛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317898_comment'></div>禅家者流，所谓「此事尚不与教乘合，而况《中庸》《大学》者」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317898_comment'></div>虽然，固有不悖于圣人者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317898_comment'></div>余每读其书，则必择其不乖戾于吾说者，时时为之钩玄撮要，而余之所未达者，则释而不推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317898_comment'></div>不推，谁其比忧，亦庄生说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317898_comment'></div>虽然，人皆企其为欢欣之乐，吾独慨其多幽忧悲咤之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317898_comment'></div>彼将悼彭祖，怜惠施，悲如驰而莫止者，哀形化而心然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317898_comment'></div>至于末篇，感时忧道，读者可为流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317898_comment'></div>然则，乐莫乐乎此书，悲莫悲乎此书！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317898_comment'></div>乐欤悲欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317898_comment'></div>足以归欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317898_comment'></div>壬午四月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317898_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　与周密唱和，有诗。作品：《次韵周公谨见寄》<div id='poem_56800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵周公谨见寄<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56800")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56800'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56800'>十年思美人，渊沦抑天飞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56800'>辛勤种青门，竟作抱蔓归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56800'>日月老宾送，霜露沾人衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56800'>沾衣何足云，八表笼烟霏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56800'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56800_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56804?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56804'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56804'>空山学仙子，满耳笙箫听。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56804_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56804'>谁知九天上，云扉本不扃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56804_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56804'>度世同御风，蓬蓬随飘零。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56804_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56804'>又如芬陀花，出火而青青。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56804_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56804'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56804_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56802?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56802'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56802'>涪翁雪堂仙，分谊故不疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56802'>投之孤芳篇，托根岂云虚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56802'>报以蟠桃实，一尝千载馀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56802'>洗髓蹑阆苑，游于物之初。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56802'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56802_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56803?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56803'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56803'>射洪高蹈翁，哀歌泪盈盈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56803'>幽居观元化，悼此岁月更。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56803'>感遇三十篇，读之慨余情。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56803'>白露号玄蝉，春日鸣仓庚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56803_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56803'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56803_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56801?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56801'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56801'>退之怀桂林，药物珍陆离。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56801'>物情恶衰歇，义心感亲知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56801'>我生欠一死，不死当语谁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56801'>与我制颓龄，悠悠白云期。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56801_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56801'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　次韵汤淑逊诗句。作品：《次韵汤淑逊谢笔墨长句》<div id='poem_56799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵汤叔逊谢笔墨长句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56799")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56799'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56799'>南屏翁，斯文千古何终穷，清辉灵气斗牛充。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56799'>我从公家二老话此事，寒更支坐烛跋红。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56799'>哀哉人琴俱亡天地覆，有刀有玉谁错砻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56799'>翁今岿然鲁灵殿，砥柱一叶万仞中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56799'>朅来访我维摩室，我起于坐欣迎公。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56799'>惊呼绝叹吾道厄，客卿颖士委蒿蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56799'>灶煤苇管不足用，宣城黟水无良工。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56799'>奈何盲卒乘钝马，欲写杰作称词雄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56799'>赠公撒雷挥电施敏手，馀事渲染<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>文字如飞虫。<div id='poem_sentence_8_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_56799'>我生哀伤所欠死，十年破砚烟雨濛。<div id='poem_sentence_9_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_56799'>一朝洗眼获玉句，金膏水碧浸方瞳。<div id='poem_sentence_10_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_56799'>翰墨场中身老大，期公盛气晚霞同。<div id='poem_sentence_11_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_56799'>峥嵘素论犹激烈，始信迂儒曲学如发蒙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_56799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_56799'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_56799_0'>⑴ 《诗渊》册二页一四七五作采弋</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_56799_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年8月19日</a>　八月，书御制御书诗后。作品：《家藏书御制御书诗恭跋》<div id='poem_1317906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317906' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317906?labeling=true' target='_blank'>家藏御制御书诗恭跋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1283年8月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317906")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317906_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317906'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317906'>臣景定壬戌以国子司业兼翰林权直，明年癸亥，以中书舍人升兼直学士院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317906_comment'></div>故事，经筵侍从官、词臣，递宿玉堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317906_comment'></div>其后浸弛，臣僚寓宿，辄称疾不入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317906_comment'></div>臣之为词臣也，恪遵旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317906_comment'></div>又明年甲子，朝廷亦申严国典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317906_comment'></div>夏六月丙辰，臣入直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317906_comment'></div>申时，中官李忠辅传旨，锡臣金香酒肆瓶、新荔枝五百颗，盖异恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317906_comment'></div>臣即援词苑旧比，具短表奏谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317906_comment'></div>翼日，遂有宸章之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317906_comment'></div>自是七月，而星文示变，玉色弗怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317906_comment'></div>十月，而先帝弃群臣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317906_comment'></div>是诗也，圣作之绝笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317906_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317906_comment'></div>痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317906_comment'></div>臣衰老，病卧山中，感世运之变迁，悼斯文之湮晦，顾瞻玉堂，如在天上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317906_comment'></div>而遁身逃难之馀，河汉天章，六丁护持，纸敝墨渝，金声玉振，臣辄装褫宝藏臣家崇奎之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317906_comment'></div>因恭诵宸篇诗《赐易简》之句，而重有感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317906_comment'></div>本朝三百馀年，崇儒右文，宠嘉词臣，赐以圣制，始于熙陵赐学士苏易简，而臣被遇穆陵，实终之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317906_comment'></div>天将丧斯文也，遗音绝响，殆止于斯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317906_comment'></div>天之未丧斯文也，回澜启秀，尚未可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317906_comment'></div>臣之子孙，其为臣宝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317906_comment'></div>癸未八月中秋后四日庚子，孤臣某百拜恭书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1317906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1283')">1283年</a>　侄子端常集其父文章，廷鸾命之为《续荆玉集》，并为序。作品：《续荆玉集序》<div id='poem_1317899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>续荆玉集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1283年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317899")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317899'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317899'>昔东坡公《与袁公济诗》云：「文如翻水成，赋作叉手速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317899_comment'></div>秋风起鸿雁，我亦继华躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317899_comment'></div>那知君蹭蹬，独泣荆山玉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317899_comment'></div>某诵而悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317899_comment'></div>苏公此言，殆为先兄发也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317899_comment'></div>兄少子端常，集其遗文成编，余欲序而藏之，而名之曰《荆玉集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317899_comment'></div>已而又读安阳韩魏公序司封之文，曰：「自淄州通判居忧，手编兄文，授其少子彦直，以《荆玉集》为名，且志兄有才而不遇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317899_comment'></div>兄之状貌言语，今不得见之矣，其得见者，平生所谓文章耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317899_comment'></div>诸子辈得不宝而惜之哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317899_comment'></div>韩公之序云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317899_comment'></div>于是合苏、韩二公之说，名吾兄之文曰《续荆玉集》，以遗其子焉，后之君子，其必有以悼之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317899_comment'></div>兄苦学，曩在京师，馆余从官宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317899_comment'></div>鸡初鸣，已秉烛操觚，或述己作，或涂抹学子所业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317899_comment'></div>朝绅与邻者窥见之，唶唶嗟叹，以厉其子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317899_comment'></div>一日自择其文若干篇，作两大轴，笑谓余曰：「此未惬吾志者，即今守门兵妇，所谓拣不中者是也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317899_comment'></div>为之绝倒，屏去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317899_comment'></div>他如己酉乡赋程文，冠乙选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317899_comment'></div>庚申、辛酉余在都曹，方有公事，兄代述沂邸讲卷，作《毛诗解》数百篇，皆靡有遗耗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317899_comment'></div>兄今在兮，文讵可期？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317899_comment'></div>兄蚤逝兮，文止于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317899_comment'></div>瘗以冢兮草木芳，泛以瓢兮波澜洋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317899_comment'></div>兄不少留兮我涕滂，咨尔巽常谨尔藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317899_comment'></div>乃命第六男端益，书其集端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317899_comment'></div>时余年六十二。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1317899_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1284&endYear=1284')">1284年</a>　正月四日，有诗。作品：《正月四日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（正月四日，为宋太祖陈桥兵变，黄袍加身之日。）</span><div id='poem_56717' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56717' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56717?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正月四日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1284年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56717")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56717_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56717'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56717'>皇厌纷拿五季馀，万兵朝遣暮还都。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56717'>虎头预卜清明旦，鳌足重开混一区。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56717'>天下归仁吾有道，日中为市尔无虞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56717'>孤臣白首怀佳节，奠桂焚兰泪与俱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56717_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56717'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56717_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1284&endYear=1284')">1284年</a>　拜母墓，作诗。作品：《过屺瞻墓》<div id='poem_56735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56735?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过屺瞻墓</a><span class='authorDate'>（1284年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56735")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56735_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56735'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56735'>白发苍颜六十三，年年拜母忆中男。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56735'>云归别岫山呈碧，江抱寒汀水染蓝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56735'>草报春晖天罔极，树随人<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作年）</span>老我何堪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56735'>荐馀煮茗清泉供，泪泫馀潸酒不酣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56735_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56735'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56735_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1284&endYear=1284')">1284年</a>　侄端巽、端常异财分关，廷鸾书后。作品：《书二侄分关后》<div id='poem_1317946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书二侄分关后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1284年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317946")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317946'>昔唐相元微之《诲侄等书》曰：「吾不能远喻他人，汝独不见吾兄之奉家法乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317946_comment'></div>吾兄半生羁游，以相给足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317946_comment'></div>吾受吾兄正色之训，感慈旨一言，逊志于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317946_comment'></div>粗成一名，吾之所得以为兄者，则汝之所得以为父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317946_comment'></div>有父如此，尚不足为汝师乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317946_comment'></div>今端巽、端常，父母俱逝，孑然独立，于世变艰难之中，不得已析薄赀，以持寒门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317946_comment'></div>此吾兄苦学所积也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317946_comment'></div>今将以微之所以诲侄者诲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317946_comment'></div>盖吾曾祖太师盘山翁，无兄弟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317946_comment'></div>吾祖太师和公，兄弟五人，而和公独当家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317946_comment'></div>诸祖意向不齐，而和公一意包容，保持门户，迄无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317946_comment'></div>吾之二父信公、朝奉公，兄弟才二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317946_comment'></div>和公既逝，吾所后信公，养母训弟，以至协比婚姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317946_comment'></div>而吾以弟之子，为兄之子，则其孝友可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317946_comment'></div>二公授馆人门，藉束脯以养其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317946_comment'></div>朝奉公病，信公亲治药具，亲携亵器，以扶持之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317946_comment'></div>生徒皆以为讶，信公正色曰：「吾弟，相依为命者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317946_comment'></div>闻者心服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317946_comment'></div>信公薨，朝奉公泣血而哭之，如哭其父；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317946_comment'></div>葬之，如葬其父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317946_comment'></div>乡人啧啧嗟悼，至今犹有能言之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317946_comment'></div>吾兄弟之相与，已不如先人多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317946_comment'></div>然亦粗有可言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317946_comment'></div>吾兄弟三人，幼孤，奋身力学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317946_comment'></div>丙午，与兄偕荐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317946_comment'></div>次年，偕上春官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317946_comment'></div>兄以耘人之财给我东上，吾独登第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317946_comment'></div>食贫五年，兄假馆养母育我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317946_comment'></div>至吾娶妇之后，有孤妹未嫁，吾捐奁财，兄捐脯资，相与聘送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317946_comment'></div>吾登朝，以至叨窃政路，势利薰人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317946_comment'></div>兄未尝以一事累我，我未尝以一辞望兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317946_comment'></div>吾抱疾去位，兄终年奔走，扶持而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317946_comment'></div>旬日，而兄迁谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317946_comment'></div>此吾所为终天之痛也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317946_comment'></div>汝等观吾兄弟相处，岂有赀产之可析乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317946_comment'></div>岂有血气之可争乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317946_comment'></div>岂有仆妾之为雀鼠、妻子之为风雨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317946_comment'></div>盖吾家三世以推梨逊枣为习尚，以易衣并食为活计，以同肝共胆为命脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317946_comment'></div>今区区薄产，关约所载，悉公悉实，无毫发可指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317946_comment'></div>顾此尺寸曾何足道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317946_comment'></div>惟是友睦一事，乃吾家万金良药，汝兄弟尚能守之，吾有以见兄于地下，是受汝之赐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1317946_comment'></div>否则，无以见先兄于地下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1317946_comment'></div>努力努力，勉之勉之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1317946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年3月11日</a>　为汪元量《湖山类稿》作序，题其集曰“诗史”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年10月</a>　十月，妻张氏卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年秋</a>　廷鸾撰成《读史旬编》，作自序。作品：《读史旬编自序》<div id='poem_1317951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读史旬编<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>自序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317951")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317951'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317951'>《读史旬编》者，病叟暮年之所著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317951_comment'></div>昔东莱吕太史著《大事记》，其为书也，曰记事，列事之目，无所褒贬抑扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317951_comment'></div>曰通释，本《易·系辞》、《书》、《诗·序》，旁采刘向、董仲舒、史迁，以及胡五峰之说，明帝王之统纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317951_comment'></div>曰解题，为始学者设，所载皆职分之所当知，非事驳杂，求新奇，出于人所不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317951_comment'></div>初公之为书，本起春秋，迄五代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317951_comment'></div>书未及成，而绝笔于汉武帝征和三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317951_comment'></div>朱文公屡惜之，伤斯文之不续，后学之不得私淑诸人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317951_comment'></div>今辄不自揆，本康节邵氏《经世》纪年图、朱文公《通鉴纲目》，略仿吕氏义例，而为《读史旬编》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317951_comment'></div>旬者，日之甲癸也，《书》曰「期三百六旬」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317951_comment'></div>吾书以日之甲癸，比于年之甲癸，谓之《旬编》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317951_comment'></div>自尧甲辰至五代周显德七年庚申<span class='inlineComment2'>（周以此年正月四日方禅。）</span>，三千三百一十七年，为三百三十二旬<span class='inlineComment2'>（末旬自甲至庚。）</span>，类而编之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317951_comment'></div>自康节先生作《皇极经世书》，纪年始唐尧甲辰，而尧之前无年可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317951_comment'></div>于是伏羲而下，至唐尧之前，本《易大传》、《家语》、《五帝德》，与夫百家言皇坟者，书其槩，以备太古之事，而谱黄帝之世焉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317951_comment'></div>又自尧甲辰以下，以至周平王己未之前<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，随年而书其事，无事则虚其年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317951_comment'></div>终之以诗书杂传所载，以备二帝三王之事，而谱夏商之世焉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317951_comment'></div>自孔子作《春秋》，编年始周平王之四十九年己未，终敬王之三十九年庚申，鲁西狩获麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317951_comment'></div>《左氏传》终贞定王元年癸酉，鲁哀公如越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317951_comment'></div>是编入春秋之后，列事目于前，《春秋》之经是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317951_comment'></div>述解题于后，凡王事、伯事之可论者著之，诸国之事不著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317951_comment'></div>其他则有《左氏》之传，诸儒之经说，不敢僣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317951_comment'></div>自司马公作《通鉴》，始周威烈王之二十三年戊寅，而威烈王戊寅之前，上距贞定之甲戌，《左传》之所不书，《通鉴》之所未续，则采刘道原《外纪》，为《传》《鉴》补遗之书，亦随年书其事，无事则虚其年，而不敢遗焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317951_comment'></div>《通鉴》战国而下，以至五代后周之前，亦列事目于前，朱公之《纲目》是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317951_comment'></div>述解题于后，效东莱《大事记》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317951_comment'></div>阅诸家之史，以广其见闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317951_comment'></div>集诸儒之说，而订其得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317951_comment'></div>若征伐之本末，制度之沿革，亦粗及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317951_comment'></div>而谱周至五季之世焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317951_comment'></div>自黄帝迄五季，其子孙之传序，已见于谱矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317951_comment'></div>汉、三国、六朝、北魏、齐、周以及五季，其疆理之离合，又为图焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317951_comment'></div>成书之首，以《通说》数条，论作史之源流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317951_comment'></div>历代之首，则以《皇极经世》数，考气运之推迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317951_comment'></div>凡此，皆职分之所当知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317951_comment'></div>而愚恨其不能尽知，且聊欲便省记也，其如孤陋寡闻何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317951_comment'></div>经始于壬午之冬，彻编于乙酉之秋，越三岁而后三十有八帙之书成，姑以备遗忘，授儿曹而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317951_comment'></div>陈了翁言《通鉴》为药山，学者惟当爱日孜孜，日游此山而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317951_comment'></div>吾老且倦游矣，东坡云：「脚力尽时山正好，莫将有限趁无穷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317951_comment'></div>唐子西亦云：「棋罢收成败，书慵卷是非」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317951_comment'></div>棋之成败，犹书之是非，罢且慵之时，收且卷之日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317951_comment'></div>窥陈编以盗窃，长兀兀以穷年，岂七十老翁事哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317951_comment'></div>虽然，是固不可不令儿辈觉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317951_comment'></div>乙酉秋浣书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1317951_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1317951'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_1317951_0'>⑴ 谱黄帝所以谱唐虞也。唐虞皆为五帝，而皆不传于子，则无可谱者。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_1317951_0'>⑵ 太史公编年，首共和庚申厉王居彘之岁月，今但以《春秋》初年为断。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1317951_0'>⑶ 唐虞既无可谱，周之世数未也，未可谱。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1317951_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年初冬</a>　作吊理宗诗。作品：甲子初冬，宿直玉堂，凄风小雨，次日即承先帝晏驾之变。距今二十年矣。大忌前一日，孤臣独眠山庵，景象正似当年。挑灯危坐，闻田家鼓笛之声，凄其有感二首。<div id='poem_56629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56629' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56629?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲子初冬宿直玉堂凄风小雨次日即承先帝晏驾之变距今二十年矣大忌前一日孤臣独眠山庵景象正似当年挑灯危坐闻田家鼓笛之声凄其有感二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年初冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56629")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56629_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56629'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56629'>无限都人哭鼎龙，年多泽久似仁宗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56629'>愁来一样黄昏雨，天上人间自不同。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56629_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56629'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56629_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56628' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56628' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56628?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1285年初冬）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56628_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56628'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56628'>云黯天低结暝阴，孤灯对影夜沉沉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56628'>可怜一曲村田乐，犹是尧民击壤音。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56628'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56628_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年</a>　端临约于是年始著《文献通考》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　葬夫人张氏于德兴县银山乡古莲塘，作墓志铭。作品：《鲁国夫人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1318008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318008' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318008?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鲁国夫人墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1318008")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318008_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318008'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318008'>夫人张氏，讳某，徽州婺源人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318008_comment'></div>曾祖盛美，将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318008_comment'></div>祖昌辰，将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318008_comment'></div>父遂，承节郎，监庆元府都作院；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318008_comment'></div>母潘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318008_comment'></div>年二十有三，归于前进士鄱阳马某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318008_comment'></div>登受封爵，郡：新安、文安、安定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318008_comment'></div>国：吉、庆、鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318008_comment'></div>生于戊子正月，殁于乙酉十月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318008_comment'></div>将葬，其夫念其子之悲，将叙而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318008_comment'></div>昔平园周公，晚而自铭其闺人，曰：「幽阴坤从，他人莫宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318008_comment'></div>况余衰老，岂复能吹寒竽之音，以寄绝弦之感乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318008_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318008_comment'></div>夫人起闻家，嫔儒族，性刚劲而实俭慈，常以佛课自律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318008_comment'></div>当承平时，营菽水奉余慈亲，抽簪珥嫁余孤妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318008_comment'></div>儿诗书，女桑麻，勤粗警细，履盈保冲，鱼轩象服不为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318008_comment'></div>晚逢世变，西移东趋，寄安托危，规深虑密，荒原野薮不为忧悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318008_comment'></div>妇人常德耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318008_comment'></div>余以弱才腐力，逢危履巇，乞身于燎原之先，灭迹于稽天之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318008_comment'></div>虽视息人间，固无以见先人于地下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318008_comment'></div>虽然，吾进之时，惟恐吾之不得退，而援之止者谁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318008_comment'></div>吾退之日，惟恐吾之复进，而尼之行者谁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318008_comment'></div>始余以文学掾登朝，列入馆，轮当面对，隔班劾去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318008_comment'></div>仓皇奉太夫人出关，夫人整比行李，独抱余奏篇以出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318008_comment'></div>大珰遣皇城逻者睨索之，不得，乃免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318008_comment'></div>国家以余东宫旧臣，引以自近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318008_comment'></div>忠为妒障，事与志违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318008_comment'></div>忧危薰心，酸辛呕血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318008_comment'></div>舆疾出，次六和塔，室无姬侍，夫人独处秀江亭上，亲为余作粥和药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318008_comment'></div>待命六十日，不得命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318008_comment'></div>再入，有旨令家人还第，夫人固留江干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318008_comment'></div>余内引，自乞暂寓太府寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318008_comment'></div>明禋，扈从恭谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318008_comment'></div>马上骨立，都人咸怜之，国家哀而许之去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318008_comment'></div>或遣余所亲，谕意夫人，宜为恩泽子孙计，出国门一步，不幸即为旅殡人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318008_comment'></div>夫人慷慨流涕谓所亲：「今所祈者惟一去耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318008_comment'></div>朝廷苛留病夫，担阁国事，即死且不偿责，何恩泽之云」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318008_comment'></div>明日，遂有书殿与祠之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318008_comment'></div>余固幸于解璁珩而挂衣冠，夫人则甚甘于释笄珈而躬井臼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318008_comment'></div>不自意既归踰年，复以越帅起家，江东祥刑使者受朝命迫余就道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318008_comment'></div>怵余行者滔滔，邀余止者寥寥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318008_comment'></div>余之出处，实为狼狈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318008_comment'></div>夫人独命小史质诸神，得阴壮阳稚之繇，命诸子延使者入卧内，视余疾，使者不得已，以疾闻，再与祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318008_comment'></div>盖自是亟上悬车之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318008_comment'></div>余固凛凛待后命，夫人怡然其适意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318008_comment'></div>异时从臣奏子授京官，癸亥端复当奏，则劝以貤恩兄子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318008_comment'></div>锁厅进士中选，试南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318008_comment'></div>甲戌端临当试，则戒其子留家尝药，不得行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318008_comment'></div>是岂薄夫荣，而羞子贵者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1318008_comment'></div>进退之际，系念深矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1318008_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1318008_comment'></div>祝柱之规弗谋，徒使倚楹之忧滋深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1318008_comment'></div>朝坐燕与者，无救于世之倾危，徒使宫居閒处者，日虞其身之颠沛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1318008_comment'></div>揭之墓门，将日引月长，君之志不可磨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1318008_comment'></div>而草没苔荒，吾之责胡可诿也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1318008_comment'></div>吾不敢使他人读之，吾子孙读之，知其非直晋潘之悼亡，而永愧于楚莱之栖遁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1318008_comment'></div>尚何言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1318008_comment'></div>生于戊子正月，殁于乙酉十月二十八日，葬以丙戌十二月壬寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1318008_comment'></div>其地在德兴县银山乡之古莲塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1318008_comment'></div>六男子：端复、端临、端履、端蒙、端颐、端益；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1318008_comment'></div>三女子：长，前卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1318008_comment'></div>幼未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1318008_comment'></div>修职郎朱焕文、从事郎费世文、太学生彭开，其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1318008_comment'></div>孙女四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1318008_comment'></div>志其墓曰「故鲁国夫人张氏」，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1318008'>古之辞公卿而乐耕钓者，其独往之风，与其偕隐之人，高矣远矣，不可及矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1318008_comment'></div>猗若冲渊，从夫君兮溯沿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1318008_comment'></div>翟茀朝兮忧则违之，裘褐归兮乐而安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1318008_comment'></div>进何必参东厢之语兮，退何必赋北门之篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1318008_comment'></div>山有木兮水有莲，与夫同藏兮伊归独贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1318008_comment'></div>谁铭新阡兮，我稽平园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1318008_comment'></div>谓余不信兮，皎日在天。</div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1318008_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年9月</a>　弟马骏孺卒，作祭文。作品：祭亡弟总幹文、九日祭亡弟总幹文。<div id='poem_1318015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭亡弟总干文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1318015")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318015'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318015'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318015_comment'></div>绍定之元，先人即世，兄才九龄，弟甫四岁，我生七年，亦未毁齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318015_comment'></div>母抱群雏，家徒四壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318015_comment'></div>画荻而教，采梠而食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318015_comment'></div>食我犹艰，教我谁即。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318015_comment'></div>维方氏姑，欲抱汝去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318015_comment'></div>曰劲斋翁，实能训汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318015_comment'></div>取诸其怀，涕零而与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318015_comment'></div>独余从兄，诗书相和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318015_comment'></div>带经而锄，饭牛而歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318015_comment'></div>每嗟予季，谋习若何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318015_comment'></div>更六寒暑，微一音邮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318015_comment'></div>母怀弗康，命我往求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318015_comment'></div>川谷之长，林涧之幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318015_comment'></div>行即其家，忽遇诸涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318015_comment'></div>鲁髽齐屦，樵牧与俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318015_comment'></div>翁耄而荒，子娱以嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318015_comment'></div>我心不决，告母还诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318015_comment'></div>又阅三霜，始勇一行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318015_comment'></div>泥涂溅溅，雨雪彭彭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318015_comment'></div>遂挟子归，俾学我傍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318015_comment'></div>束书授徒，负箧从兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318015_comment'></div>简编之乐，弦诵之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318015_comment'></div>或鸡三号，或夜参半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318015_comment'></div>忘食已晡，烯薪欲旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318015_comment'></div>我擢儒科，弃此兔园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318015_comment'></div>子自衿奋，鱼跃于渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318015_comment'></div>我官江圻，去此东冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318015_comment'></div>子自婚媾，凤求其凰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318015_comment'></div>戊午初荐，我留家巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318015_comment'></div>奸回曰丁，以痴物相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318015_comment'></div>合者冥升，背者远放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318015_comment'></div>其人虎视，其党睢盱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318015_comment'></div>啧有烦言，慑处愁居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318015_comment'></div>子于此时，而奉乡书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318015_comment'></div>辛酉再荐，我列朝绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318015_comment'></div>便嬖曰林，以吠犬狺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318015_comment'></div>请诛履斋，欲媒其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318015_comment'></div>我对延和，细为上陈：「本朝家法，不杀大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318015_comment'></div>无滑此手，以伤吾仁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318015_comment'></div>一言蹇蹇，万目睽睽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318015_comment'></div>爱我者我奇，怒我者我麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318015_comment'></div>子于此时，而荐胄闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318015_comment'></div>谓为获伸，再进再踬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318015_comment'></div>谓为不逢，孰凭孰翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318015_comment'></div>以贤能献书，以门品授秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318015_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318015_comment'></div>命乡论秀，一第崎岖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318015_comment'></div>惟有司不明，国舍虞比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1318015_comment'></div>一官拓落，而天下无邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1318015_comment'></div>既中年之郁郁，又晚岁之皇皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1318015_comment'></div>伊寒门之撑拄，与浊世而低昂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1318015_comment'></div>姑忍尤而攘垢，孰投簪而搴裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1318015_comment'></div>忽号山穷，乃熟黄粱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1318015_comment'></div>临绝之音，一何琅琅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1318015_comment'></div>曰怀抱其靡终，以妻子为余累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1318015_comment'></div>念子平生，诸缘略备，婚嫁毕图，儿孙孔峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1318015_comment'></div>先人之绪业未荒，姑氏之蒸尝有继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1318015_comment'></div>倘颓龄之关天，可含笑而入地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1318015_comment'></div>维昔之时，老不哭少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1318015_comment'></div>何今之衰，兄哭其弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1318015_comment'></div>昔兄之亡，三人行而损一人，于《易》为《损》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1318015_comment'></div>今弟之殁，二惠竞而弱一个，于传为危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1318015_comment'></div>有文以觞，无泪可挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1318015_comment'></div>如身无臂，如车无軏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1318015_comment'></div>孤鸿失侣独啼云，长庚孤明不陪月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1318015_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1318015_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_67_1318015_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318016' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318016' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318016?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九日祭亡弟总干文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1318016")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318016_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318016'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318016'>维著雍困敦之岁，无射之月，亡弟总干止堂君三年制终，将以良月祓除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318016_comment'></div>其兄某乃以萸菊之辰，奉糕酒之奠，别灵筵而告之曰：呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318016_comment'></div>古人有言，閒居爱重九之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318016_comment'></div>今我不乐，独立无同气之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318016_comment'></div>嗟余季之冥升，阅黄花之三零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318016_comment'></div>始而枕棺外舍，中而设几中庭，终而隙驹迅驰，祥琴成声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318016_comment'></div>吾寡兄弟，而弗忍也，孰敢违先王之礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318016_comment'></div>然则，酒能浇胸中之磊块，菊能制短世之颓龄乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318016_comment'></div>感物思人兮涕泗横，慨今怀昔兮寝梦惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318016_comment'></div>吾尝与君，奉母齐山，江涵秋影，欣然适携壶之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318016_comment'></div>又尝与君，从兄东府，风吹松竹，恻然感对床之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318016_comment'></div>或霜螯左持，或云液细倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318016_comment'></div>今辰何辰，酌此醁醽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318016_comment'></div>故吾今吾，视此伶俜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318016_comment'></div>矧终年之大病，将鬼趣而人形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318016_comment'></div>腹彭亨而不能纳膻馨，足拥肿而不能踰柴荆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318016_comment'></div>嗟若君存，能不我矜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318016_comment'></div>余又安能登高望远，临流叹逝，睇汝君山之阳，而视汝白云之京也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318016_comment'></div>灵兮何之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318016_comment'></div>魂兮何营？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318016_comment'></div>将为浮沤为飞尘，弃我捐我，即九原之昏昏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318016_comment'></div>抑为祥云为庆星，福我寿我，驱二竖于冥冥乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318016_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318016_comment'></div>「明年纵健人应老，昨日追欢意已迟」，非东坡《九日怀子由》之赋乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318016_comment'></div>「鸿雁池边照双影，鹡鸰原上忆三人」，非涪翁《九日怀知命》之句乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318016_comment'></div>彼怀兮一时，吾怀兮千古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318016_comment'></div>缀辞写哀，有泪如雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318016_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318016_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1318016_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　作记。作品：《净土院舍田记》<div id='poem_1317991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>净土院舍田记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317991")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317991'>院更唐宋，且将五百年，前人之述备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317991_comment'></div>盖尝以檀法度人，施者无翼而翔，不踵而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317991_comment'></div>当乾道辛卯，有初施田者，僧真悟大师道崇丐文于吾伯祖潜溪翁，翁为说偈言云：「信心生供养，念起即无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317991_comment'></div>我田无穷年，我福亦无尽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317991_comment'></div>自后迨今百有十六年，由朱君纯仁而降，长者李公以建殿及诸佛菩萨像施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317991_comment'></div>毛君自任以建三门、创弥陀殿施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317991_comment'></div>王君曰平夫、曰立夫以金刚像施；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317991_comment'></div>曰宰、曰彬之、曰立夫，又皆以田施。<div class='inline'
