id='poem_sentence_7_1317991_comment'></div>而余兄弟暨昭文、文忠、南康公，又皆以题扁施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317991_comment'></div>凡施之事，田为大院之僧如本宏、普顺、普润者，皆肃肃然奉其教，无敢越规矩准绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317991_comment'></div>且将修彼之礼以耕之，陈彼之义以种之，讲彼之学以耨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317991_comment'></div>于是又介吾犹子，奉潜溪翁遗文，谒余而请记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317991_comment'></div>余观多田翁尽东其亩，祖也传之孙，三世希不失矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317991_comment'></div>父也传之子，再世希不失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317991_comment'></div>孰能更千百年不坏、不灭，如浮屠氏之为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317991_comment'></div>潜溪翁之言，验于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317991_comment'></div>虽然，谓僧而可无田乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317991_comment'></div>则彼之人，固自为大言曰：「我师之教尽虚空，遍法界皆吾福田耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317991_comment'></div>释迦云：与大比丘千二百五十人，俱乞食王舍城中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317991_comment'></div>王舍城，即吾田也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317991_comment'></div>国一师领径山千馀众，寺无常产，庖廪不继，山之神龙，实助缘化，山龙即吾田也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317991_comment'></div>吾之田，若恒河沙数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317991_comment'></div>历僧祇劫，是可限以顷亩，裁以岁月乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317991_comment'></div>谓僧而可有田乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317991_comment'></div>则吾之人又律以正论曰：梵居者僧，野耕者民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317991_comment'></div>必也复而室家，还而冠巾，而后畀而田畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317991_comment'></div>室家之不复，冠巾之不还，而田畴是畀，僧而民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317991_comment'></div>民而僧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317991_comment'></div>虽然，姑舍是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317991_comment'></div>僧之祈余曰：吾因檀施助缘，建弥陀诞节，修西方净土胜缘，其田得米三十斛有奇，是所为谒记者也夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317991_comment'></div>随其心净，则佛土净，此净土说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317991_comment'></div>我无秽行之稊稗，人获无量之果报，此福田说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317991_comment'></div>施福田，修净土，庸何讥焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317991_comment'></div>彼将慊于不耕而食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317991_comment'></div>于是取檀施之田，自耕而食之，以逃吾人之讥可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317991_comment'></div>古德云：「诸方说禅，浑浑何似？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317991_comment'></div>我怕饥种田」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317991_comment'></div>此语真实有味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317991_comment'></div>或问莘郊乐尧舜之道于某禅师，答曰：「江上一犁春雨，良以耕食凿饮，道在其中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317991_comment'></div>于吾儒之说，未大戾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317991_comment'></div>姑以是文之，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1317991_comment'></div>后之观文者，将无谓其附会空玉之谈乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1317991_comment'></div>抑亦不乖圣人之道乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1317991_comment'></div>是未可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1317991_comment'></div>安得起潜溪翁于九原，再拜而质之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1317991_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年</a>　留梦炎为元吏部尚书，招马端临，以父老辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年</a>　题方景云书稿。作品：《题方景云课稿后》<div id='poem_1317934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题方景云课藁后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317934")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317934'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317934'>余与景云同生于壬午，同荐于丙午，有二同之契焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317934_comment'></div>由丙午至于今，四十有二年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317934_comment'></div>景云之为人笃实，其文尔雅而深纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317934_comment'></div>场屋之作，非直灵于己，其所沾溉，辄复高列荐名中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317934_comment'></div>间试太常，不奏第，余之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317934_comment'></div>初与典举，冬烘遂失景云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317934_comment'></div>每诵东坡《与李方叔诗》，为之永叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317934_comment'></div>盖其首章曰：「与君相从非一日，笔势翩翩疑可识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317934_comment'></div>平生漫说《古战场》，过眼终迷日五色」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317934_comment'></div>余固尝以是愧景云也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317934_comment'></div>其末章曰：「买羊沽酒谢玉川，为我醉倒春风前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317934_comment'></div>归家但草凌云赋，我相夫子非臞仙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317934_comment'></div>余又不知夫世变至此，不复可以是期景云也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317934_comment'></div>悲哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317934_comment'></div>然景云泊然，不以望我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317934_comment'></div>暇日，抄其所为文，成一钜编，示余，且曰：「其书数语，示我子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317934_comment'></div>惟毋引李方叔云」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317934_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317934_comment'></div>吾经五十八篇，可命题者何限？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317934_comment'></div>作者何限？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317934_comment'></div>其在于今，惟张才叔一篇，可为痛哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317934_comment'></div>余之罪，岂惟失一景云而已！</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1317934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年3月</a>　三月，撰其远祖马燧家传，题其后。作品：《题太傅北平莊武王家传后》、北平家传成。<div id='poem_56712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北平家传成<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>编首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56712")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56712'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56712'>三百年间事屡危，降之人杰岂中衰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56712'>巍巍祖烈将千岁，赫赫元功彼一时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56712'>起义堂碑云汉丽，凌烟阁像日星垂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56712'>藏山自纂前朝史，付与云礽百代知。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56712_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56712'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56712_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56713?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>辨谤</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56713_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56713'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56713'>选将初年起范阳，和戎晚节误平凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56713'>大功宜受春秋责<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作赏）</span>，盛毁何能日月伤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56713'>文士谈兵多谬误，兰台作史漫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>裁量。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56713'>折衷自有成书在，公论从知千岁长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56713'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_56713'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_56713_0'>⑴ 《诗渊》册六页四二○五作狡童誉父妄</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_56713_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_56714' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56714' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56714?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>感事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56714_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56714'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56714'>彼美人兮无古今，挑灯勘史夜沉沉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56714'>昌唐无复浯溪颂，哀郢常多楚泽吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56714'>麟获自伤王迹息，鹃啼谁念帝魂深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56714'>祇今莫唱贞元曲，但忆曾闻正始音。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56714_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56714'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56714_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题太傅北平庄武王家传后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317929")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317929'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317929'>右《唐太傅北平庄武王家传》二卷，二十一世孙某采前史，修成一编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317929_comment'></div>惟先王勋德在前朝，赞述在史官，其子孙无敢以拟议为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317929_comment'></div>然自唐、南唐至本朝，阅代者三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317929_comment'></div>自贞元乙亥至于今丁亥，阅年者四百九十有二矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317929_comment'></div>某不幸当本朝倾覆，中华沦陷，悲宗社之陵夷，愧祖风之轶坠，悼往谋之不臧，伤后咎之谁执？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317929_comment'></div>昔韦玄成诗责躬，而述绥殷傅楚之前劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317929_comment'></div>庾子山赋《哀江南》，而叙承周佐汉之旧绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317929_comment'></div>所感而起，固所以为书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317929_comment'></div>书成，诵《黍离》之三章，而流涕以识其后云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317929_comment'></div>彊圉大渊献季春中浣前二日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1317929_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年9月9日</a>　重九，为王氏甥诗集作序。作品：《王甥儒珍集序》<div id='poem_1317900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王甥儒珍集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317900")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317900'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317900'>王甥典谟之学，蚤有声场屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317900_comment'></div>科举废，辄敛才华而为诗，政尔精丽可喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317900_comment'></div>暇日，手抄此编示余，余读其《精卫行》及说杭事等篇，皆绰绰有诗人风致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317900_comment'></div>昔徐东湖为山谷从甥，山谷一见东湖诗，便勉进步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317900_comment'></div>古人甥舅间以诗道相切磋如此，余老，不能进于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317900_comment'></div>甥之齿未也，抽尔秘思，骋尔妍词，异时齿宿意新，当伟然为一大家数！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317900_comment'></div>渠家半山老人之诗曰：「解我葱珩脱孟劳，暮年甘与子同袍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317900_comment'></div>新诗比旧增奇峭，若许跻攀莫大高」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317900_comment'></div>余之解葱珩、脱孟劳久矣，展我甥兮，尚洗眼以观奇峭之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317900_comment'></div>丁亥重九。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1317900_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年11月</a>　友人、姻娅向伯恭卒，作墓志。作品：《总领秘撰费君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1318002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>总领秘撰费君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1318002")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318002'>余读《诗》至《匪风》之末章，曰：「谁将西归，怀之好音」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318002_comment'></div>未尝不泫然流涕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318002_comment'></div>盖东周而西怀者，岐丰之士大夫，文、武、成、康之遗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318002_comment'></div>国家玉斧画河，眷焉殿西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318002_comment'></div>异时拓天扶日，盖出西豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318002_comment'></div>过江百年，岷峨悽怆，扶携保旅而南者，可以侨置东益州矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318002_comment'></div>矧复与荆吴泯泯一息，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318002_comment'></div>公费氏，汉丞相后，讳伯恭，字希吕，世为成都人，庄简公之孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318002_comment'></div>本儒家子，迁房为贵公孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318002_comment'></div>所后贵轩公，以儒术为西州大帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318002_comment'></div>蜀难，携家南下，以编简从纨裤，以俊选造秀侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318002_comment'></div>丙午拔漕荐，不第，俯就京秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318002_comment'></div>初筮为西饷官属，再调浙西帅司酒官，转东饷干官，辟主管文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318002_comment'></div>自国家多事，戊己云屯，庚癸日呼，饷掾无他，鞭算而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318002_comment'></div>公检防钱粟，补苴罅漏以赞其长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318002_comment'></div>由是无师不宿饱之虞，而有军无乏兴之喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318002_comment'></div>顷入宰浦城，浦城，闽壮邑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318002_comment'></div>邑政宜民，民咸安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318002_comment'></div>公尝为余言：「邑民甚醇，吾政多暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318002_comment'></div>尝晚步阅廛俗，以验吾政否臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318002_comment'></div>则父老辄持茗碗，为长官寿，熙熙然父子如也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318002_comment'></div>吴雨岩，号为当世吏师，闻风纳交，复欲以饷所辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318002_comment'></div>会公除京帑外补，贰郡三山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318002_comment'></div>三山帅府，贵寓森立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318002_comment'></div>有名卿尝以事抵公府，公当官而行，无所阿徇，卿为愧谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318002_comment'></div>曰：「不如是，何以为南府判」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318002_comment'></div>《会计录》之作，俾来者稽以为验，于郡计有功焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318002_comment'></div>当坚边设候之时，擅治法征谋之选，沿江制副治九江，公参其军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318002_comment'></div>府罢，辄奉朝命兼摄诸司，列校风从，三军凫藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318002_comment'></div>公所调娱多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318002_comment'></div>由是守蕲、摄黄、守舒，以至司江庾，护淮漕，领西饷，皆雄司也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318002_comment'></div>朝廷不至，用违其才，公则所至，官修其方，材可为时不可为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318002_comment'></div>公涖官雄剧，受任艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318002_comment'></div>排山倒海，而扁舟独航；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318002_comment'></div>破柱倾梁，而孤木横支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318002_comment'></div>难乎，不难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318002_comment'></div>其间关而英簜是移，则遁尾之厉，不敢辞也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318002_comment'></div>其缱绻而羁绁以从，则灭顶之凶，不遑避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318002_comment'></div>要亦臣子一至之分而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318002_comment'></div>鼎迁物改，公由闽而鄞，而杭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318002_comment'></div>畴昔西山南浦之间，尔宅尔田，不堪回首矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318002_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318002_comment'></div>明夷伤也，伤于外者，反于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318002_comment'></div>公既违《大易》之序矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318002_comment'></div>鸿飞遵渚，公归无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318002_comment'></div>于汝信处，吾敢忘诗人之意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318002_comment'></div>挽公来鄱，种秫东皋，结茆西塾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318002_comment'></div>松风万壑，意及而文哀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318002_comment'></div>夕阳西流，破涕而为笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1318002_comment'></div>余与公同之，忘其吴蜀之隔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1318002_comment'></div>居无何，暴客讧旅琐之巢，伏戎抄丰蔀之屋，两家资用荡析。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1318002_comment'></div>余守先人坟墓，不能去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1318002_comment'></div>家人女妇辈，偕公依邑廛以居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1318002_comment'></div>公与人有情，于物无著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1318002_comment'></div>时僚邑士，皆乐从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1318002_comment'></div>乙酉冬，余悼亡，公来吊甚哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1318002_comment'></div>留止信宿，乃谓余曰：「吾丘墓遐思，则枕簟馀潸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1318002_comment'></div>在蜀者远不能寻，在洪者老不能往」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1318002_comment'></div>因放声长号，余亦不知涕泗之横集也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1318002_comment'></div>讵料阅岁馀而公已无意于斯世耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1318002_comment'></div>夫人杨氏，平舟公女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1318002_comment'></div>一子世文，妇马氏，余中女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1318002_comment'></div>孙山孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1318002_comment'></div>公殁之日，丁亥五月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1318002_comment'></div>葬以其年十一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1318002_comment'></div>得吉卜于余里之宜斯园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1318002_comment'></div>自世变以来，蜀客皆莫知其所往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1318002_comment'></div>独前温陵谭侯应斗，与公里人，相好而居相近也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1318002_comment'></div>谭侯之状公行也，事有源流，辞无枝叶，足以传矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1318002_comment'></div>世文砻石速铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1318002_comment'></div>昔余在中书，公驱驰外服，稔其才猷，因与来往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1318002_comment'></div>余避贤病归，旧雨无踪，而偃月有萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1318002_comment'></div>公乃拳拳以其子请昏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1318002_comment'></div>余惟恐累公，公顾欲亲我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1318002_comment'></div>生，于我乎亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1318002_comment'></div>殁，于我乎铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1318002_comment'></div>余后公死，尚何辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1318002_comment'></div>尝闻蜀叟言，庄简公当韩氏专国时，其独立也，不可得而戚疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1318002_comment'></div>其勇退也，不可得而系维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1318002_comment'></div>公在边效命之秋，正在廷擅事之日，其心平识远，有庄简之遗风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1318002_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_1318002'>岷峨之西中大江，真人玉斧画我疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1318002_comment'></div>异才间出骇四方，紫岩拔起宾太阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1318002_comment'></div>虞赵诸公蔚相望，朝辞剑阁暮岩廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1318002_comment'></div>公之先祖简且庄，燮调大化参翱翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1318002_comment'></div>百年人物尽圭璋，故家乔木扶明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1318002_comment'></div>蜀雨其濛四表荒，吴天来下万里航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1318002_comment'></div>司土子人靖我邦，飞刍挽粟峙乃粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1318002_comment'></div>悠悠苍天一星黄，大厦如倾谁栋梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1318002_comment'></div>黍离麦秀神内伤，兰摧桂折人云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1318002_comment'></div>公不少留我涕滂，钻石埋辞永公藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_89_1318002_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　建小楼于林居之后，储书其上，读书其下，命曰老学道院，作《记》作品：《题老学道院》<div id='poem_56678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题老学道院<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56678")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_56678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56678'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56678'>天典民彝圣得知，斯文千岁以为期。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56678'>试看涑水三雍赞，何必兰陵赋诡诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56678'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56678_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56840?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_56840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56840'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56840'>瓜烂东陵老废锄，野民八十尚耽书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56840'>窗风文字翻叶叶，抱膝长吟一拥炉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56840'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56840_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56838?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_56838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56838'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56838'>白日临晨老可娱，平生有味太玄𤕠<span class='inlineComment2'>（豫章本作符）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56838'>莫将华皓嗤童习，更采玄文扁此庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56838'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56838_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56839?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_56839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56839'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56839'>繁笔泉石两成痴，早学东家晚学西。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56839'>章甫峨峨宁汝误，如今翻恨十年迟<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《碧梧玩芳集》卷二四）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56839'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56839_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　为族子作字说。作品：《族子德淳字说》<div id='poem_1317950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>族子德淳字说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317950")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317950'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317950'>族弟之子德淳，生于乙丑，其纪年为咸淳初元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317950_comment'></div>长而工医，其学为太仓令淳于公之学，德淳请序于余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317950_comment'></div>余曰：汝以其生之年，则淳为咸淳之淳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317950_comment'></div>以其学之业，则淳为淳于公之淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317950_comment'></div>姑因汝之业，制汝之字，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317950_comment'></div>宜以「子全」字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317950_comment'></div>《周官》医师之职，十全为尚，十失一次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317950_comment'></div>问臣意：「诊病决死生，能全否乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317950_comment'></div>对曰：「意治病，先切脉，心不精脉，所期死生，时时失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317950_comment'></div>臣意不能全也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317950_comment'></div>德淳必也能全《周官》之十全，而又能全淳于公之不能全，是为青于蓝、寒于水，可以托人性命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317950_comment'></div>人之言曰：「老医少卜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317950_comment'></div>医何必老？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317950_comment'></div>史称秦越人得方于长桑公、太仓令得方于唐里公孙，皆自少时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317950_comment'></div>公孙之授仓公，亦曰：「吾身已衰，无所复事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317950_comment'></div>是吾年少所得妙方也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317950_comment'></div>医何必老？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317950_comment'></div>顾慧性何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317950_comment'></div>夫医非慧男子不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317950_comment'></div>慧则通，通则神，圣工巧出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317950_comment'></div>侄之齿未也，而其性专静，其学精审，殊有老成之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317950_comment'></div>吾病夫也，吾贫于黎庶，而医傲于王公，幸其族有人，则朝夕吾门，视吾病，诊吾脉，吾以身试之，良验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317950_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317950_comment'></div>子全勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317950_comment'></div>吾年五十一罢归，鬓须之焦黄久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317950_comment'></div>今抱沉痛，年六十有七，几死者数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317950_comment'></div>倘非饮我上池之药，则汝伯何由发如漆也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317950_comment'></div>书以为德淳字说。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317950_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　作轩，命曰遗老轩，并为《记》作品：遗老轩记。<div id='poem_1317995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>遗老轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317995")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317995_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317995'>苏黄门辅政于元祐，谪官于绍圣，归居于崇宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317995_comment'></div>诸子为之筑庐颍滨，其自言曰：「吾颍滨遗老也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317995_comment'></div>尝自谏官，不五年与闻国政，虽号为得志，而实不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317995_comment'></div>今退居杜门，不与物接，心之所可，未尝不行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317995_comment'></div>心所不可，未尝不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317995_comment'></div>行止未尝不如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317995_comment'></div>平生之乐，莫过今日」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317995_comment'></div>苏公之所谓「遗老」者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317995_comment'></div>晋秘书少监徐广，东莞人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317995_comment'></div>刘氏易代之际，广悲感流涕，或责之曰：「徐公得无少过」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317995_comment'></div>广曰：「君为宋朝佐命，身是晋室遗老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317995_comment'></div>悲欢之事，固不可同」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317995_comment'></div>徐公之所谓「遗老」者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317995_comment'></div>然则一遗老也，乐莫乐乎颍滨，悲莫悲乎东莞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317995_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317995_comment'></div>要亦各适其适而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317995_comment'></div>从容乎老桧修竹之间，啸傲乎凤台平湖之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317995_comment'></div>避事已谢客，养性不看书，苏公之所为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317995_comment'></div>守丹徒之坟墓，怀京口之桑梓，八龄手不释卷，一岁遍读五经，徐公之所为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317995_comment'></div>有士于此，壮误恩华，晚逢倾覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317995_comment'></div>其始也类苏公之不如意，而无其晚岁之乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317995_comment'></div>其终也类徐公之不可同，而有其暮年之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317995_comment'></div>于是家有林亭，箧存竹素，亦妄以「遗老」自名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317995_comment'></div>于二公宜何择焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317995_comment'></div>曰：吾进难企乎颍滨，是犹倾而未颠之初也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317995_comment'></div>《易》曰：「履霜坚冰，阴始凝也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317995_comment'></div>苏公之时以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317995_comment'></div>退已堕乎东莞，是固沦胥以亡之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317995_comment'></div>《玄》曰：「海水群飞，蔽于天航」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317995_comment'></div>徐公之时以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317995_comment'></div>为苏公不可，舍徐安归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317995_comment'></div>抑二公，皆八十馀老，则造物之所赋厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317995_comment'></div>士当踰六垂七之年，久生何益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317995_comment'></div>饰巾待终而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317995_comment'></div>不然，则古之人有上相誇荣，中台耀宠，时开一卷，时饮一杯，老而自乐，何乐如之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317995_comment'></div>盖自名曰「长乐老」矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317995_comment'></div>然而斥以寡廉，登之杂传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317995_comment'></div>国则兴亡相继，身则富贵自如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317995_comment'></div>欧阳公、司马公耻之，士亦耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317995_comment'></div>是为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1317995_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　作跋。作品：《题赵德亮诗论后》<div id='poem_1317925' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317925' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317925?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题赵德亮诗论后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317925")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317925_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317925'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317925'>著雍困敦之岁，青阳载熙，积阴骤霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317925_comment'></div>玩芳病叟读《易》至《未济》终焉，而庐山赵德亮，远以其《删诗要论》来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317925_comment'></div>叟扶病读之，抚而叹曰：深乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317925_comment'></div>德亮之为是书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317925_comment'></div>其援据精，故其说辨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317925_comment'></div>其感慨极，故其味长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317925_comment'></div>或曰：「郑康成以《三礼》笺《诗》，儒者未之许也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317925_comment'></div>今君以《春秋》评《诗》，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317925_comment'></div>余应曰：不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317925_comment'></div>《诗》、《春秋》，皆史也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317925_comment'></div>《序》之言曰：「国史明乎得失之迹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317925_comment'></div>以《春秋》评《诗》，讵谓不然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317925_comment'></div>六经惟《诗》、《春秋》当自其变者观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317925_comment'></div>康衢之谣，虞廷之歌，果《诗》之本始乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317925_comment'></div>《诗》之兴也，谅不于上皇之世，先儒有是言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317925_comment'></div>达事怀旧，俗诗之所为作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317925_comment'></div>君著《诗论》，以为仲尼删《诗》于鲁哀公之十一年，而作《春秋》于十四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317925_comment'></div>其事相因，不偶然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317925_comment'></div>谓非自其变者观之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317925_comment'></div>是故观风者不徒观之《周南》、《召南》，观于《豳风》《下泉》之思可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317925_comment'></div>观雅者不徒观之《文王》、《大明》、《绵》，观于《荡》之伤、《旻》之闵可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317925_comment'></div>观颂者不徒观于《猗》、《那》、《清庙》，观于正考父之犹能存商、季孙行父之犹请命于周可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317925_comment'></div>否则，成汤、高宗、微子之云为，文、武、成、康、周、召之规制，岂如弁髦而因以敝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317925_comment'></div>盖人心之全经，与天壤相敝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317925_comment'></div>《诗》之兴，非世变云乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317925_comment'></div>《诗》之存，独世变云乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317925_comment'></div>变在彼，不变在我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317925_comment'></div>故曰：「发乎情，民之性也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317925_comment'></div>止乎礼义，先王之泽也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317925_comment'></div>又曰：「皓天不复，忧无疆也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317925_comment'></div>千岁必反，理之常也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317925_comment'></div>「四始」之孰是孰非，《大序》之为得为失，糟粕而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317925_comment'></div>齐、鲁、韩、毛束高阁，独抱遗经究终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317925_comment'></div>于是藏之名山，以待后之学者，足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317925_comment'></div>昔孔氏作《春秋》，九月而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317925_comment'></div>卜之得阳豫之卦，未知删《诗》之后，卜之得何卦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317925_comment'></div>君如通其说，尝试以语我来。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1317925_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　白鹿洞书院修复，作记。作品：《庐山白鹿洞书院兴复记》<div id='poem_1317992' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317992' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317992?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山白鹿洞书院兴复记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317992")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317992_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317992'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317992'>谨按国史，淳熙八年十一月辛丑，礼部言：知南康军朱熹奏：「庐山白鹿洞书院，在本军星子县界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317992_comment'></div>恭闻先朝尝赐之国子监九经，又尝敕有司重加修缮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317992_comment'></div>考此山佛老之祠以百数，兵乱之馀，次第兴葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317992_comment'></div>而先王礼乐之宫，所以为化民成俗之本者，乃反寂寥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317992_comment'></div>臣蒙恩假守，始即其故基，度为小屋，教养生徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317992_comment'></div>欲望继述两朝神圣遗意，特降敕命，仍旧以白鹿书院为额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317992_comment'></div>诏国子监仰摹御书石经，印造《九经注疏》、《论》、《孟》等书给赐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317992_comment'></div>事下国子监勘当，监上礼部奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317992_comment'></div>从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317992_comment'></div>于是东莱吕成公为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317992_comment'></div>后三十有八年，南康守臣重修，而勉斋黄公记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317992_comment'></div>又后十有六年，江东宪臣重修，而蒙斋先生袁公记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317992_comment'></div>后五十有四年，斋藏不戒于火，百年儒宫，一夕湮灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317992_comment'></div>斯文之厄极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317992_comment'></div>于是领生徒、尸讲席者，䀌然动心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317992_comment'></div>任藩侯为师帅者，慨然出力，披荒拨烬，度材鸠工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317992_comment'></div>爰畀之人徒焉，赋之财粟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317992_comment'></div>旧日规制，乃大兴复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317992_comment'></div>入其境，则山葱茏，水汩㶁者，文公之旧也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317992_comment'></div>登其门，则夏屋渠渠，章甫峨峨者，文公之旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317992_comment'></div>且于微阐显幽之馀，更有饰回增美之观，斯亦奇矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317992_comment'></div>山长某姓等，写图纂事，授简于鄱阳后学马某，而俾记其成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317992_comment'></div>某避席曰：呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317992_comment'></div>大川为陵，平陆成江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317992_comment'></div>师亡友散，法烂道穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317992_comment'></div>文公之学，有如弁髦，而因以敝之矣，谈何容易！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317992_comment'></div>昔公之托记于东莱氏也，言言而商订，句句而裁量，惟恐一语之差，将变秀才为学究，而随缘说法，应病与药者之无以传无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317992_comment'></div>于是，成公之告学者，则欲挹先儒淳固质实之馀风，服《大学》离经辨志之始教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317992_comment'></div>于以寻关洛之绪言，而惩荆舒之陋习焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317992_comment'></div>已而勉斋之记，壹是皆以治心修身为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317992_comment'></div>蒙斋之记，三致意于正谊明道之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317992_comment'></div>是皆大儒先生之格言大训，后学无复措一辞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317992_comment'></div>今姑述兴复之本末而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317992_comment'></div>抑诸君游文公之学，登其堂，伏其几，袭其裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317992_comment'></div>亦尝读其书，而诵其赋乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317992_comment'></div>赋之末，言公吃紧为人处也，曰：「诚明其两进，抑敬义其偕立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317992_comment'></div>允莘挚之所怀，谨颜巷之攸执」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317992_comment'></div>诵斯言者，不过曰志伊学颜而已，愚以为未尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317992_comment'></div>挚之怀，亦曰莘郊乐尧舜耳，不必幡然而改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317992_comment'></div>颜之执，亦曰陋巷甘箪瓢耳，不必用之则行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317992_comment'></div>诚能怀于斯，执于斯，抱坚白如玉雪，抗青紫于浮云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1317992_comment'></div>由是藏焉，修焉，游焉，息焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1317992_comment'></div>宇宙一窗，圣贤千载，或凄凉经醉石之傍，或慷慨感卧龙之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1317992_comment'></div>当其抚以深怀，得无有招余新好者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1317992_comment'></div>宜谢之曰：吾之业，在《洞赋》之终篇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1317992_comment'></div>倘幸以为可，则愿刻诸石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1317992_comment'></div>若曰辞列三先生之次，有荣耀焉，则某何敢僭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1317992_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　题饶娥庙。作品：《饶娥庙记》<div id='poem_1317993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饶娥庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317993")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317993'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317993'>娥立节唐宝应壬寅，更五代暨先朝，迄于今五百二十有七年，历壬寅者八矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317993_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317993_comment'></div>唐于此时，银貂纵横，王室如燬，妖狐起仆，河朔为墟，斯六阴之穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317993_comment'></div>而有贞女子，行烈丈夫事，独于吾州邑见之，幽姓而节亘千年，荒江而名振八表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317993_comment'></div>斯昭昭者岂偶然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317993_comment'></div>制书之赐于唐者一，于先朝者一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317993_comment'></div>石章之立于唐者二，于先朝者八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317993_comment'></div>自娥立节以来，八年而祠与碑立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317993_comment'></div>二十年而唐制书初下，柳河东之碑继立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317993_comment'></div>百一十年而废碑再立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317993_comment'></div>二百一十六年而先朝邑官碑阴有记；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317993_comment'></div>又三十四年而宋景文之史有书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317993_comment'></div>又十五年而迁庙立，有碑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317993_comment'></div>又百六十年而别庙立，有碑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317993_comment'></div>又二十一年而先朝制书再下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317993_comment'></div>褒表者，节义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317993_comment'></div>自娥立节以来，百有一十年而初祠焚，前碑燬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317993_comment'></div>又四百有六年而别庙焚，众碑悉燬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317993_comment'></div>废兴者，时变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317993_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317993_comment'></div>节义贯天地，时变自古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317993_comment'></div>纲三常五，宁同榱桷以俱焚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317993_comment'></div>天典民彝，岂与瓦砾以偕烬！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317993_comment'></div>譬如众星分耀，日毂冥濛，有时而阳耀大明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317993_comment'></div>四渎争流，沧溟浩渺，有时而鲸浸洞开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317993_comment'></div>又安知无恻怛勤民，慷慨望古，为之兴仆植僵者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317993_comment'></div>盖娥之英烈，地行为神，空飞为仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317993_comment'></div>或搴月窟之芳，使士之舒翘扬英者叩焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317993_comment'></div>或洒天瓢之霖，使农之植稻种黍者祈焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317993_comment'></div>于是别庙焚、群碑毁之十年，当彊圉大渊献之岁，邑人稽赞府应公分祠东山之始谋，踵文元杨公迁祠邑西之旧规，而新大之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317993_comment'></div>其明年三月壬子首事，六月庚辰落成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317993_comment'></div>前筑月台，中敞殿宇，丹雘粲然，鼓钟炉案备具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317993_comment'></div>祠之初建也，有白犬伏神座下，依依终日，投之鱼肉不食，齧灰而去，不知所之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317993_comment'></div>岂异时娥感父尸，固有衔机梭之祥，而厖也复出于斯时欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317993_comment'></div>吁嗟厖兮，彼固进不得拟桃花，以扈嵩洛之涂车刍灵，退犹得附黄苍，以彰吴越之义夫烈妇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317993_comment'></div>生斯时，睹斯异者，欲不流涕叹息于斯，而不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317993_comment'></div>于是士民相与授简于里之病叟，而记其成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317993_comment'></div>娥之烈，前人之述备矣，无复谆谵赞一辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1317993_comment'></div>姑详废兴以纪时，述幽灵以感物而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1317993_comment'></div>病叟者，卧中条山，久幽不死，而名不称焉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1317993_comment'></div>叟既成文，又作迎享送神三章，俾歌以祀焉，而并刻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1317993_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1317993'>日吉兮辰良，芳菲菲兮满堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1317993_comment'></div>蕙殽烝兮兰藉，奠桂酒兮椒浆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1317993_comment'></div>灵连蜷兮既留，烂昭昭兮未央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1317993_comment'></div>驾飞龙兮于征，邅吾道兮乡之长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1317993_comment'></div>波滔滔兮泪盈盈，望汾潭兮磐石横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1317993_comment'></div>仙滩兮扬灵，扬灵兮未极隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1317993_comment'></div>思君兮太息，朝驰骛兮江之浔，夕弭节兮县西之侧，待娥不来兮使我心恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1317993_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1317993'>我生之初尚无为，我生之后唐世衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1317993_comment'></div>有父溺死兮谁者怜之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1317993_comment'></div>呼天与地兮涕涟洏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1317993_comment'></div>至险不测涛与风，至幽不仁鱼与龙，至孝不昧感即通，岂人之灵兮不若厖之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1317993_comment'></div>惟天地之无穷兮，哀吾生之弱龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1317993_comment'></div>往者吾不及兮，来者吾不获观其败与赢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1317993_comment'></div>愚公老矣山为平，精卫藐然海为倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1317993_comment'></div>枕吾戈兮縳尔缨，猛志毅气妖氛澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1317993_comment'></div>昊天克巩兮靡人弗胜，诵娥之烈兮摇我心旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1317993_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1317993'>自我天覆，云之油油。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1317993_comment'></div>大田多稼兮，屯膏是忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1317993_comment'></div>雄虹朝隮兮，雌霓夕虬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1317993_comment'></div>触石兮通气，雷车兮电帜，雨甚至兮神哉沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1317993_comment'></div>农有成功兮，怀鸡黍之招邀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1317993_comment'></div>士未失职兮，冀鹏鲲之扶摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1317993_comment'></div>锡之丰岁兮，俾尔馀饶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1317993_comment'></div>报以修程兮，匪我宣骄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1317993_comment'></div>扬桴兮拊鼓，饯飙游兮远渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1317993_comment'></div>欲少留此灵琐兮，日忽忽其将暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1317993_comment'></div>祝娥之来下兮，慰我士民于终古。</div><div id='poem_sentence_67_1317993_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年9月9日</a>　重九，作祭弟马骏孺文。作品：《九日祭亡弟总幹文》<div id='poem_1318016' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318016' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318016?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九日祭亡弟总干文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1286年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1318016")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318016_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318016'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318016'>维著雍困敦之岁，无射之月，亡弟总干止堂君三年制终，将以良月祓除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318016_comment'></div>其兄某乃以萸菊之辰，奉糕酒之奠，别灵筵而告之曰：呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318016_comment'></div>古人有言，閒居爱重九之名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318016_comment'></div>今我不乐，独立无同气之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318016_comment'></div>嗟余季之冥升，阅黄花之三零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318016_comment'></div>始而枕棺外舍，中而设几中庭，终而隙驹迅驰，祥琴成声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318016_comment'></div>吾寡兄弟，而弗忍也，孰敢违先王之礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318016_comment'></div>然则，酒能浇胸中之磊块，菊能制短世之颓龄乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318016_comment'></div>感物思人兮涕泗横，慨今怀昔兮寝梦惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318016_comment'></div>吾尝与君，奉母齐山，江涵秋影，欣然适携壶之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318016_comment'></div>又尝与君，从兄东府，风吹松竹，恻然感对床之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318016_comment'></div>或霜螯左持，或云液细倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318016_comment'></div>今辰何辰，酌此醁醽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318016_comment'></div>故吾今吾，视此伶俜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318016_comment'></div>矧终年之大病，将鬼趣而人形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318016_comment'></div>腹彭亨而不能纳膻馨，足拥肿而不能踰柴荆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318016_comment'></div>嗟若君存，能不我矜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318016_comment'></div>余又安能登高望远，临流叹逝，睇汝君山之阳，而视汝白云之京也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318016_comment'></div>灵兮何之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318016_comment'></div>魂兮何营？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318016_comment'></div>将为浮沤为飞尘，弃我捐我，即九原之昏昏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318016_comment'></div>抑为祥云为庆星，福我寿我，驱二竖于冥冥乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318016_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318016_comment'></div>「明年纵健人应老，昨日追欢意已迟」，非东坡《九日怀子由》之赋乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318016_comment'></div>「鸿雁池边照双影，鹡鸰原上忆三人」，非涪翁《九日怀知命》之句乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318016_comment'></div>彼怀兮一时，吾怀兮千古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318016_comment'></div>缀辞写哀，有泪如雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318016_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318016_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1318016_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　友人、姻娅李雷应卒，端临求为其岳父作墓志铭。作品：《大监李君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1318003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大监李君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1318003")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318003'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318003'>子应姓李氏，讳雷应，鄱浮邑人，忠靖公长子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318003_comment'></div>公经学流声，如川沄沄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318003_comment'></div>文字行世，如日杲杲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318003_comment'></div>君含英咀华，舒翘擢干，经之传人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318003_comment'></div>孔明盛心，尝受任于艰危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318003_comment'></div>士行晚岁，不婆娑于绵笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318003_comment'></div>君内典机筹，终躬办护，家之钜子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318003_comment'></div>榻前论奏，本狐突教子之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318003_comment'></div>边头耕桑，有庆州似父之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318003_comment'></div>王之荩臣，邦之良翰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318003_comment'></div>由太学上舍生登进士第，由郡文学赞征西幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318003_comment'></div>内历馆、寺、郎、监，外累擢刺史二千石，往往皆光绍先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318003_comment'></div>一旦韬辉沈馨，与时徂谢，惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318003_comment'></div>子弟力学，而幼悟夙成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318003_comment'></div>博闻强记，有耆儒宿士所不能知者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318003_comment'></div>儒科入仕，而绝塞穷边，兵屯师律，有老校退卒所不能言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318003_comment'></div>余尝举君以不如，而又戢君良箴者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318003_comment'></div>延和之对，知其不肯以售脂韦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318003_comment'></div>湟中之籴，知其不忍以侔茧丝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318003_comment'></div>晋阳之垒，知其不肯以隳保障也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318003_comment'></div>其末也，人皆闭户，君且缨冠，良欲藉通材以靖本邦而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318003_comment'></div>《易》曰「遁亨，遁而亨也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318003_comment'></div>「小利贞，浸而长也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318003_comment'></div>古人区区未极之间，图其暂安，而为所屑为，盖《易》之教也，尚何言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318003_comment'></div>问其年不登中寿，问其秩不踰列大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318003_comment'></div>自名司显位，既不获展其未用之蕴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318003_comment'></div>而荒原断涧，又不获老其不遇之年，亦独何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318003_comment'></div>人伦生死，大幻也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318003_comment'></div>世事新陈，大梦也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318003_comment'></div>中外历职，大彩选也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318003_comment'></div>官曹决事，大杂戏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318003_comment'></div>作是观者，名为大观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318003_comment'></div>君质迈气灵，必有超然于此者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318003_comment'></div>君之弟若子，孝敬人也，能谱君年日月可考；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318003_comment'></div>君之友，直谅人也，能状君行事实不诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318003_comment'></div>其爵里之详，其世祚之远，其宅兆之安，彼谱若状具矣，铭无以为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318003_comment'></div>余之仲子，实为君婿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318003_comment'></div>一日归白其父曰：「外舅病中说大人常在口，意将属大人铭，大人勿辞也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318003_comment'></div>忆昨余读书徐岩山中，与东涧汤公考评南渡初中原故老之遗文，观其叙婚姻，述乡邻，伧荒陆沉，死生契阔，凄然在目，未尝不读而悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318003_comment'></div>至云龛李公酹其亲家马大夫之文，曰：「丧乱而来，同郡几人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318003_comment'></div>若已脱之须髭，与将晓之天星」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318003_comment'></div>当时东涧为之讽诵不已，余年未三十，叵信此境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318003_comment'></div>柰何三纪之馀，悲又甚也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318003_comment'></div>余与君，姓偶同前人，君又少余七岁，乃不能以此文酹我，反援此铭君，又可悲之甚也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318003_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1318003'>君材博修，石渠之书可䌷乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318003_comment'></div>君志澄清，湘水之槎可乘乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318003_comment'></div>渝城之边柝可停，武昌之江垒可倾乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318003_comment'></div>蚤营四方兮惟我独贤，晚专一壑兮嗟我未老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318003_comment'></div>君之所存者要未尝亡也，孰谓亡者之不如生乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1318003_comment'></div>茫茫九原，谁能起之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1318003_comment'></div>起而莫起，斯石纪之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1318003_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　拜母墓，作诗。作品：《过屺瞻夜赋》<div id='poem_56773' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56773' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56773?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿屺瞻夜赋<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 id='poem_title_56773_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56773'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56773'>咿轧篮舆度晓岑，抚今怀昔泪淋淫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56773'>蓼莪老去仍追诵，常棣新来又废吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56773'>有恨台瓜随蔓尽，无情涧藻与波沉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56773'>僧窗月苦夜无寐，莫咏儿寒动母心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56773'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56773_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56772' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56772' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56772?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1288年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56772'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56772'>六十年前我已孤，婴儿抱母泣呱呱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56772'>昊天罔极幽明隔，良月就盈今昔殊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56772'>云塞断行悲独雁，风林反哺感群乌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56772'>澄江只似洹河水，一碧寒泓照白须。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56772'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56772_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　廷鸾卒。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京（江宁）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='98f0704ce06443fdb72e0cc9f5140f0a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("98f0704ce06443fdb72e0cc9f5140f0a");'><span id='98f0704ce06443fdb72e0cc9f5140f0a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>，26岁</div><div id='98f0704ce06443fdb72e0cc9f5140f0a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　赴省试途中，一日道间馁甚，就村居买螺蛳羮，泡蒲囊中冷饭食之，遂得胃疾。无力治药，朋友怜之者，以二陈汤服之，良愈。<br /></div>
-----end

杭州（临安）

<div class='label1' id='46b0f3e03f0242caba872221329c40bd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("46b0f3e03f0242caba872221329c40bd");'><span id='46b0f3e03f0242caba872221329c40bd_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　廷鸾入京主管户部架阁，掌档案。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　子马端临生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　为太学录，题家传四印五章。作品：《题四印五章后》<div id='poem_1317935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题四印五章后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317935")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317935'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317935'>先人往年侍亲宦游旴江，一日，叔父驰书为言，欲以勤、谨、和、俭为保家四印，先人欣然是之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317935_comment'></div>因为发明其义，成五章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317935_comment'></div>某幼孤，先人文字散落，表兄李先生，我之自出，乃能收拾序藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317935_comment'></div>既而以遗编见授，则五章者其首也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317935_comment'></div>会某录辟廱，时先生亦薄游辇下，乃掇取，手抄为此卷，以归于先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317935_comment'></div>或者当世名公钜人，见而取焉，赐之语，以为先训不朽，则亦不肖孤之至望也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1317935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　召试馆职，试策极言“强君德，重相权，收直臣，防近习”，讥及外戚、内侍，迁秘书省正字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　尤焴提举史事，辟为史馆校勘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　廷鸾素廉直，不附权贵，当轮对，丁大全命王持垕先察廷鸾意，及侯对殿门，格不得见。翼日，被监察御史朱燿劾罢归。夫人张氏抱其奏篇出城。轮对稿传于京师，廷鸾名重天下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　文天祥举进士第一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　徐霖父卒，廷鸾作诗挽之。作品：《挽徐朝奉》<div id='poem_sentence_1_56768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56768'>谏草频尊主，绯花与显亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56768_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年</a>　吴潜入相，召为校书郎。作品：《除校书郎谢吴丞相启》<div id='poem_1317860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1317860'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317860'>四年去国，甘负耒于西畴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317860_comment'></div>一旦起家，忽䌷书于东观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317860_comment'></div>天启清明之日，地回凝冱之春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317860_comment'></div>拜手知归，委心露谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317860_comment'></div>伏念某萎蕤末学，坎𡒄孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317860_comment'></div>蚤缘俊造之科，滥跻宏达之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317860_comment'></div>群飞肃肃，鹭于下以有辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317860_comment'></div>独行睘睘，虱其间而何补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317860_comment'></div>愆尤所积，摈斥是宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317860_comment'></div>遮西日以望长安，惆怅钓竿之手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317860_comment'></div>乘天风而去蓬岛，飘零槁叶之身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317860_comment'></div>尘痕自拂于莱衣，欢意孰谋于义檄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317860_comment'></div>讵期抆拭，遂许跻攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317860_comment'></div>昔怜唐士之稚狂，敢言朋字？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317860_comment'></div>今愧汉京之大雅，而理秘文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317860_comment'></div>入则有辞，以白其大人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317860_comment'></div>出则幽衡，自齿于下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317860_comment'></div>所惭短浅，莫报洪深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317860_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官柄国元臣，经邦魁宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317860_comment'></div>妙手药膏肓之疾，横身支宇宙之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317860_comment'></div>地老天荒，哀众芳之憔悴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317860_comment'></div>乾旋坤转，提独笔以陶镕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317860_comment'></div>载惟小草之微，一出大钧之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317860_comment'></div>爨桐焦尾，初辱赏音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317860_comment'></div>笼鹤剪翎，又烦刷翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317860_comment'></div>纵匪锥囊之颖出，要为箧牍之旧藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317860_comment'></div>如恐失之，亟其取耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317860_comment'></div>范公轩鉴之下，谁毁谁誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317860_comment'></div>和氏衣钵之传，不进不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317860_comment'></div>逮处中，无两月之久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317860_comment'></div>首将上，在几人之间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317860_comment'></div>试观知己于寻常，谁有我公之一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317860_comment'></div>某慨怀恩遇，锐激懦衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317860_comment'></div>念国士抢攘之秋，养人材暇豫之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1317860_comment'></div>青藜夜炯，稍窥前哲之藩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1317860_comment'></div>翠袖天寒，欲验后凋之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1317860_comment'></div>其为衔戢，罔既编摩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1317860_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1317860_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年</a>　廷鸾弟骏孺应试礼部，因丁大全把持仕路，未第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年</a>　廷鸾兼沂靖惠王府教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年3月</a>　廷鸾疏论董宋臣，贬之。兼权枢密院编修官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年</a>　廷鸾兄代作沂靖王府讲稿《毛诗解》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年</a>　贾似道入朝，功高势盛，廷鸾未尝依附。廷鸾轮对，以“遏恶扬善，举直错枉”谏。祀明堂，进诗颂。母段氏封太孺人。作品：《恭进明堂大礼庆成诗》、《仰和皇太子殿下明禋庆成诗韵》<div id='poem_56786' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56786' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56786?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恭进明堂大礼庆成诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1260年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56786")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_56786_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56786'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56786'>钜典崇邦祀，精禋展国阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56786'>泰元神授筴，癸亥日宣光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56786'>艺祖郊天始，高皇受命长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56786'>后庚基再造，先甲迓殊祥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56786'>率育歌时夏，仪刑咏我将。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56786_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
