《诗渊》册六页四四九一作六</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_56824_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　廷鸾不安于内，一再乞外补，不许。论贡举，议荒政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　廷鸾擢军器监兼左司，廷兼太子右谕德。作品：兼右谕德辞免奏状。<div id='poem_1317834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兼右谕德辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317834")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317834'>自天有命，蹐地无容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317834_comment'></div>臣窃以圣主诒谋，莫重元良之本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317834_comment'></div>儒臣劝讲，尤严赞谕之僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317834_comment'></div>孰谓谫材，遽尘华选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317834_comment'></div>伏念臣蠢愚下士，迂狷诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317834_comment'></div>久污班行，已寸长之蔑取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317834_comment'></div>骤登储寀，于三善以何裨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317834_comment'></div>忽蒙黼扆之简知，躐预青宫之讽导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317834_comment'></div>载稽唐制，见谓优秩清班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317834_comment'></div>允若圣时，率用名流胜士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317834_comment'></div>臣既无素望，又匪旧人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317834_comment'></div>特被选抡，殊骇观听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317834_comment'></div>惧深维谷，谊合循墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317834_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，俯鉴愚悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317834_comment'></div>收回命渥，免陪春诵之联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317834_comment'></div>别选才良，上辅日新之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317834_comment'></div>庶安愚分，仰答隆恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317834_comment'></div>所有恩命，臣未敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317834_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1317834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　升左谕德，行国子司业。作品：除兼国子监司业辞免奏状、再辞免国子监司业申省状、除国子司业谢庙堂启。<div id='poem_1317835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除国子监司业辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317835")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317835'>自天有命，蹐地无容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317835_comment'></div>伏念臣才不如人，学未闻道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317835_comment'></div>侥逾里选，靡由庠序以进身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317835_comment'></div>缀缉时文，莫识圣贤之用意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317835_comment'></div>有若儒官之选，允由士类所推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317835_comment'></div>况朝廷天宽地大之时，正学校鱼跃鸢飞之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317835_comment'></div>欲淑佩襟之仪表，是资领袖之端良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317835_comment'></div>有如乐正之官，是曰司成之副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317835_comment'></div>阳城可谓有道，乃见服于学徒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317835_comment'></div>高闶岂非儒臣，或贻讥于公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317835_comment'></div>仰寻先哲，内惧非才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317835_comment'></div>倘犹昧于循墙，将有叱而避席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317835_comment'></div>辄殚微悃，仰冒皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317835_comment'></div>恭望圣慈，俯照忱恳，收回误渥，改畀时流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317835_comment'></div>大学得名儒，使羞其行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317835_comment'></div>师氏教国子，永观厥成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317835_comment'></div>所有恩命，臣未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1317835_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317855?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再辞免国子监司业申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1262年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317855")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317855_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317855'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317855'>鼎来明制，震惕危衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317855_comment'></div>窃以乐正抡材，儒官典教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317855_comment'></div>不模不范，充员甫愧于摄承；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317855_comment'></div>如丝如纶，误渥旋叨于特置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317855_comment'></div>已惭曳组，敢复滥巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317855_comment'></div>伏念某近被优恩，遽尘清选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317855_comment'></div>君之仁者善养士，方将崇化厉贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317855_comment'></div>臣之壮也不如人，何以典乐教胄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317855_comment'></div>谫才无取，威命有严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317855_comment'></div>共二任于一身，不能者止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317855_comment'></div>未三旬而再命，其谓斯何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317855_comment'></div>有鹈翼之不濡，无皋比之可彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317855_comment'></div>恩深识拔，谊合控辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317855_comment'></div>伏望朝廷特赐敷奏，收回宸命，改畀名流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317855_comment'></div>官惟其人，然后英才育而天下喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317855_comment'></div>教必以正，庶几师道立而善人多。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1317855_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除国子司业谢庙堂启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1262年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317867")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317867'>元良天下本，首参审谕之联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317867_comment'></div>太学贤士关；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317867_comment'></div>复贰成均之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317867_comment'></div>两极儒绅之荣遇，一由公衮之殊知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317867_comment'></div>无遏尔躬，不濡其翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317867_comment'></div>古者皇储世胄，学本一途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317867_comment'></div>王宫国都，教无二致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317867_comment'></div>是以《文王世子》之记，与夫周典师氏之官，教胄参于训储，谕德同于诏美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317867_comment'></div>师儒之选，哲乂是求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317867_comment'></div>如某者朴樕小才，啁啾短喙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317867_comment'></div>元元本本，深惭大雅之洽闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317867_comment'></div>暖暖姝姝，宁识古人之大体？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317867_comment'></div>曾微薄技，可厕清流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317867_comment'></div>入学招诸生，列属记八年之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317867_comment'></div>执经侍太子，蒙恩才数月之新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317867_comment'></div>胡然一朝，叨此二命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317867_comment'></div>既序升于鹤禁，仍躐进于虎门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317867_comment'></div>笔砚扫除，久矣失邯郸人之步；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317867_comment'></div>丝纶狎至，居然恭正考父之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317867_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官道蕴丘轲，勋高旦奭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317867_comment'></div>羽翼成矣，赞皇家贻孙子之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317867_comment'></div>股肱喜哉，得君子育英才之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317867_comment'></div>肆令妙简，并及迂儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317867_comment'></div>进宜增星辉之重，退则益海流之富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317867_comment'></div>生有笑于列者，退之不见斥于宰臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317867_comment'></div>君之职止是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317867_comment'></div>士逊将有惭于国老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317867_comment'></div>誓坚素节，用报鸿私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317867_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　廷鸾授经毕，获转官，乞赠生父。作谢执政启。作品：《回授官赠生父谢庙堂启》<div id='poem_1317862' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317862' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317862?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回授官赠本生父谢庙堂启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1262年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317862")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317862_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317862'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317862'>授经《麟趾》，猥叨懋赏之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317862_comment'></div>辄诵《蓼莪》，辄援貤恩之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317862_comment'></div>荷公朝之优许，出上宰之曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317862_comment'></div>坯冶一陶，载铭九壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317862_comment'></div>伏念某起从孱陋，适际休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317862_comment'></div>冠缨既列予府僚，倚席仍兼于邸讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317862_comment'></div>为穆生设醴，有愧谈经之儒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317862_comment'></div>见帝尧于羹，粗陈稽古之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317862_comment'></div>甫竟百篇之旨，骤跻一秩之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317862_comment'></div>辄控哀衷，妄攀曲例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317862_comment'></div>汉武功爵级，尚闻移与于父兄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317862_comment'></div>唐公辅元臣，亦有自陈于君上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317862_comment'></div>史著生亲之礼，经垂报复之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317862_comment'></div>虽圣朝画一之章，曲从忠厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317862_comment'></div>盖天下在三之义，所谓纲常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317862_comment'></div>恩彻幽泉，德均化地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317862_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官，大猷经远，盛德迈伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317862_comment'></div>丰芑孙谋之贻，永扶国栋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317862_comment'></div>《葛藟》王族之庇，更迪宗标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317862_comment'></div>载推锡类之仁，庸广因亲之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317862_comment'></div>永惟兴廉举孝之盛世，士皆有感于鸢鱼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317862_comment'></div>则凡念先报本之私情，人岂不如于豺獭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317862_comment'></div>假之误宠，徇厥微忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317862_comment'></div>某敢不仰戴洪私，益坚素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317862_comment'></div>父兮生我，既承雨露之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317862_comment'></div>主尔忘身，尚竭涓尘之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317862_comment'></div>其为衔荷，罔既敷棻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1317862_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　轮对，主治身，养心。兼翰林权直。作品：除兼翰林权直辞免奏状、再辞免翰林权直申省状、除翰林权直谢庙堂启。<div id='poem_1317836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317836?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除兼翰林权直辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317836")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317836'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317836'>恩擢超踰，愚衷震惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317836_comment'></div>切以明时掌制，聿严内命之司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317836_comment'></div>圣主抡材，尤遴外庭之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317836_comment'></div>若稽史牒，谨简词臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317836_comment'></div>官清儤直，则备自有唐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317836_comment'></div>资浅摄承，则昉由我宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317836_comment'></div>上规开宝，文郁乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317836_comment'></div>近接淳熙，道粲然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317836_comment'></div>聿求宗匠，俾典禁林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317836_comment'></div>然而望实未孚，神祖尚难于苏轼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317836_comment'></div>官名初建，孝皇始命于端诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317836_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以诸生，起于下国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317836_comment'></div>识穷短绠，无能汲古学之渊源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317836_comment'></div>思涩寒竽，不足协斯文之律吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317836_comment'></div>以场屋孱儒之靡，列缙绅华选之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317836_comment'></div>从太子游，已惧罔功于谕导；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317836_comment'></div>见王者志，若为有补于讨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317836_comment'></div>矧耆儒宿老，甫尔请归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317836_comment'></div>乃新学小生，居然代匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317836_comment'></div>纵承人乏，岂及臣愚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317836_comment'></div>恭望圣慈，俯怜卑悃，收回误渥，改畀名流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317836_comment'></div>庶几词章足以恢人文，诏令足以宣皇泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317836_comment'></div>坦然帝制，复还二典之醇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317836_comment'></div>大哉王言，俾达万民之悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317836_comment'></div>庶安愚分，用竭忱辞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1317836_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317856?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再辞免翰林权直申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1262年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317856")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317856_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317856'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317856'>言之无文，讵堪视草？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317856_comment'></div>令弗惟反，未许循墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317856_comment'></div>忱辞愿彻于四聪，愚悃遂致其再渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317856_comment'></div>伏念某以时文应举，安能为廊庙之言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317856_comment'></div>以经学窃科，岂必有词章之技？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317856_comment'></div>中岁浮沉，偶尘班路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317856_comment'></div>平生梦寐，敢望词林？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317856_comment'></div>地禁职亲，谁不艳夜炬分光之宠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317856_comment'></div>才悭思涩，或致贻春船上水之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317856_comment'></div>倘昧一辞，立呈百短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317856_comment'></div>岂独抱鹈梁之愧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317856_comment'></div>直将贻鳌禁之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317856_comment'></div>伏望朝廷，特赐敷奏，亟回误渥，别付能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317856_comment'></div>才难不其然，况值夔、龙之盛际；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317856_comment'></div>辞达而已矣，宜须班、马之名流。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1317856_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除翰林权直谢庙堂启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1262年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317868")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317868'>材惭视草，忽谬点于禁林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317868_comment'></div>恩误转钧，辄叙陈于翘馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317868_comment'></div>有愧客卿之对，难酬国士之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317868_comment'></div>伏念某读书作章句儒，应举为义理学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317868_comment'></div>青宫璧水，智逾效于一官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317868_comment'></div>金马玉堂，梦敢游于四禁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317868_comment'></div>煌煌昭代，嶷嶷宗工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317868_comment'></div>适大手笔之祈閒，简他学士而代匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317868_comment'></div>兼官两制，并命一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317868_comment'></div>招鸿鹄之群，与家鸡而作对；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317868_comment'></div>拔鹍鹏之翼，傅斥鴳以奚宜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317868_comment'></div>既莫逃春船上水之嘲，奚敢恋御烛分光之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317868_comment'></div>至如摄直，尤号才难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317868_comment'></div>当孝皇之命端诗，肇新厥职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317868_comment'></div>由淳熙而至嘉定，才用几人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317868_comment'></div>恭惟某官身荷乾坤，手抉云汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317868_comment'></div>中书草可汗之诏，赞皇公政须自为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317868_comment'></div>朝廷培翰苑之才，韩魏国裁其骤用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317868_comment'></div>既栽培于善类，欲兴起于斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317868_comment'></div>朝有老儒，王多吉士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317868_comment'></div>众工善运，然后天下称相之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317868_comment'></div>巧匠旁观，乃令吾徒掌帝之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317868_comment'></div>自惭晚出，遽冒新荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317868_comment'></div>某敢不益懋厥勤，恪恭乃服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317868_comment'></div>翰林逼华盖，顾浅闻无绾诰之长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317868_comment'></div>泰阶陈六符，岂平世有掣铃之警？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317868_comment'></div>长怀有感，短喙莫容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317868_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　廷鸾擢秘书少监，权直学士院。作品：除权直学士院辞免奏状。<div id='poem_1317837' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317837' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317837?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除权直学士院辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317837")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317837_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317837'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317837'>璧水充员，无补明时之造士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317837_comment'></div>蓬山列事，况遭圣代之右文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317837_comment'></div>仍叨叠组之荣，重误疏纶之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317837_comment'></div>非天曷戴，无地自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317837_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以孤生，起于下国，绳枢瓮牖，曾无藻色之工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317837_comment'></div>金马石渠，早愧芸香之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317837_comment'></div>顷从农亩，召复旧班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317837_comment'></div>学浅资轻，屡丐一麾于江海；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317837_comment'></div>年除岁擢，浸成三入于瀛洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317837_comment'></div>更以常才，猥参少令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317837_comment'></div>岂直今世，人文不轻得此；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317837_comment'></div>政使先朝，宿老尚或难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317837_comment'></div>惟昔淳熙，有臣必大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317837_comment'></div>尝贰职于中秘，兼典制于内庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317837_comment'></div>彼其独擅儒宗，矧又奋由词学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317837_comment'></div>然观避疏，犹云才技之无堪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317837_comment'></div>暨睹训词，凛然名实之有戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317837_comment'></div>是知华选，难畀庸流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317837_comment'></div>臣词华敢企于前儒，愚戆不逮于世事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317837_comment'></div>倘冒殊恩而亟拜，滋误睿主之选抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317837_comment'></div>俯庸披露于血忱，仰乞收回于汗涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317837_comment'></div>庶安旧次，免累圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317837_comment'></div>所有上件恩命，臣未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1317837_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　本年有诗。作品：《秘省和刘左司韵》<div id='poem_56831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秘省和刘左司韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1262年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56831")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56831'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56831'>三年三揖壁奎星，当日曾登著作庭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56831'>大雅重逢君子聚，斯文还属圣人兴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56831'>倚天延阁缘云上，拔地方壶历级升。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56831'>自别青藜仙分隔，借书独对短檠灯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56831'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56831_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>　廷鸾母段氏封太令人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年2月1日</a>　正月元旦，廷鸾擢起居舍人兼太子右庶子兼国史院编修官、实录院检讨官。作品：元日除起居舍人辞免奏状。<div id='poem_1317838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元日除起居舍人辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317838")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317838'>涣扬宸渥，震惕愚衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317838_comment'></div>切以柱下清官，朝中盛选，致君尧舜，执简操笔，皆圣人之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317838_comment'></div>事为《春秋》，广记备言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317838_comment'></div>斯国史之体，谅非长德，曷畀庸流？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317838_comment'></div>臣才望至卑，资历尤浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317838_comment'></div>复来七日，中秘首尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317838_comment'></div>泰内三阳，右螭尾进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317838_comment'></div>岁月无几，旦暮辄迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317838_comment'></div>率由典常，最称遴选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317838_comment'></div>诸所记注，尚多摄承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317838_comment'></div>若径冒于真除，重贻讥于躐进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317838_comment'></div>而况谋猷，内告缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317838_comment'></div>惭直方之姿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317838_comment'></div>书法后观，无以传深微之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317838_comment'></div>皆于圣代为有慊，夫岂愚分之所安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317838_comment'></div>与其拾级以升，徒有疾颠之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317838_comment'></div>孰若循墙而避，庶几初服之修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317838_comment'></div>恭望睿慈，不嫌改命，收回误宠，别畀时才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317838_comment'></div>式严君举之书，上赞帝王之治。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1317838_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　四月，皇太子生日，作贺诗。作品：皇太子生辰诗三首（其二）<span class='inlineComment2'>（《皇太子生辰诗三首》其二（癸亥），见《碧梧玩芳集》卷二十二，舒大刚《马廷鸾马端临父子合谱》未著录此诗。）</span><div id='poem_56823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56823")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56823'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56823'>苍龙见天东，房驷拱辰北。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56823'>煌煌心星前，炳炳天王侧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56823'>休符协乾文，正阳毓紫<span class='inlineComment2'>（《诗渊》作垂）</span>极。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56823'>铜楼蔼祥光，玉卮奉愉色。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56823'>叹声沸笙鸾，寿龄指箕翼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56823'>何以祝元良，勉哉崇明德。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56823'>学问日就将，福禄时万亿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56823'>永侍帝宸尊，重晖照四国<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：癸亥。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56823'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_56823_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　入奏，以激励人才、虚心纳言、重视邦本、谨严边备为言。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年7月20日</a>　时欲召董宋臣，廷鸾谏阻之。理宗卒用董宋臣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　史称廷鸾荐士二十人，进中书舍人。升兼直学士院。作品：除中书舍人辞免奏状、再辞免奏状、中书舍人谢上表。<div id='poem_1317839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除中书舍人辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317839")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317839'>九重超擢，孤士震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317839_comment'></div>伏念臣素拙文辞，尤疏学术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317839_comment'></div>终年鳌禁，曾无起草之工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317839_comment'></div>一日薇垣，骤玷为真之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317839_comment'></div>此何官也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317839_comment'></div>臣敢兼之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317839_comment'></div>自周典之掌赞书，是资华国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317839_comment'></div>至唐人之有还诏，亦谓回天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317839_comment'></div>词章蹇浅，则主德无以宣明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317839_comment'></div>风力销沈，则公论难乎满惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317839_comment'></div>至如真授，尤号优迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317839_comment'></div>臣修不试文而除，臣轼自记言而拜，彼皆何等材分？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317839_comment'></div>孰能与之跻攀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317839_comment'></div>厥今圣主有从谏转圜之明，诸臣多会文切理之彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317839_comment'></div>取之下品，恐不中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317839_comment'></div>倘少昧于控辞，是自贻于颠踣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317839_comment'></div>仰祈睿察，特反误恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317839_comment'></div>不嫌销印之难，择人改畀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317839_comment'></div>庶免斲窗之丑，为时起羞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1317839_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除中书舍人再辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317840")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317840'>控辞误渥，首虞掌制之非工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317840_comment'></div>尚閟俞音，更惧滥官之速戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317840_comment'></div>重殚庸陋，频渎圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317840_comment'></div>伏念臣山林之癯，本无薄技；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317840_comment'></div>岁月之近，遍历华途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317840_comment'></div>晋贰蓬山，俄接螭坳之步；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317840_comment'></div>随群鸳鹭，躐追豹尾之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317840_comment'></div>在于典常，已越夷等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317840_comment'></div>愚臣玩日，曾莫效于涓埃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317840_comment'></div>圣主如天，才一吐其狂瞽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317840_comment'></div>若更超擢，允极侥踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317840_comment'></div>士有常心，然后礼义廉耻之与立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317840_comment'></div>官既易得，正缘公卿侍从之可图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317840_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下察其愚衷，赐之圣断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317840_comment'></div>收回恩命，改畀时名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317840_comment'></div>使无处众人之所争，而多取天下之公器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317840_comment'></div>庶安愚分，永戴皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317840_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1317840_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书舍人谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1263年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317845")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317845'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317845'>载笔右坳，记事已叨于假宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317845_comment'></div>演纶西掖，代言忽冒于真除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317845_comment'></div>对金莲炬以增惭，佩紫荷囊而不称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317845_comment'></div>非天曷戴，无地自容<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317845_comment'></div>窃以修饰讨论，赞书体重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317845_comment'></div>温醇深润，典制才难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317845_comment'></div>于昭明堂，迪惟今日，宜有高文大册，以扬伟绩宏休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317845_comment'></div>巍巍乎，荡荡乎，惟尧有成功也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317845_comment'></div>浑浑尔，灏灏尔，下周其必谁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317845_comment'></div>如臣者，吹本滥竽，汲惟短绠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317845_comment'></div>结绶寖踰于四载，滥巾何意于九迁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317845_comment'></div>辞宰掾，佐儒官，蜕簿书之凡质；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317845_comment'></div>点禁林，贰秘府，陪文士之英游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317845_comment'></div>官僚徒采如春华，柱史蔑闻于辰告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317845_comment'></div>讵期睿奖，更玷亲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317845_comment'></div>六学士，三舍人，何敢望一时之名胜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317845_comment'></div>四三王，六五帝，若为兼两制之发挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317845_comment'></div>难酬雨露之恩，交积渊冰之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317845_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下圣神天造，刚健日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317845_comment'></div>河西颂天子之明，能见万里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317845_comment'></div>山东感武夫之听，迄济中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317845_comment'></div>良由号令，罔有不臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317845_comment'></div>匪独文章，焕焉可述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317845_comment'></div>斧藻益彰于圣作，网罗顾及于臣愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317845_comment'></div>命服斯皇，恩纶有炜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317845_comment'></div>臣敢不恪共官次，感诵君仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317845_comment'></div>敕经凤阁鸾台，献替无裨于大义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317845_comment'></div>名列鸡翘豹尾，论思合罄于小忠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317845_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　为外兄张氏作记。作品：《緑山胜概记》<div id='poem_1317987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绿山胜槩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1263年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317987")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317987'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317987'>婺源斗入万山间，山之邻吾境者，联岚含晖，夸奇竞秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317987_comment'></div>予外兄张君辄得其胜处居之，园于居之傍，曰「绿山胜槩」，而命记于余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317987_comment'></div>观其池亭洁修，林壑美秀，则不必丛花茂木之荫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317987_comment'></div>直栏横槛，烟霞澄鲜，则不必重闳邃宇之居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317987_comment'></div>晓窗夜檠，诗书娱乐，则不必丝竹管弦之奏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317987_comment'></div>园之胜固已各陈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317987_comment'></div>今夫士生天地间，其攀名梯，奔利航，而竭蹙不休者，欲暂而有此胜，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317987_comment'></div>厥有拄笏西山，寄径终南，而居心不静者，又安能长有此胜乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317987_comment'></div>君胸中洞然，表独立于群欢辈嚣之上，方且餐松风，饮菊露，制芰荷之衣，纫芷兰之佩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317987_comment'></div>山凡水俗，变为清辉，积李崇桃，坐览葩丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317987_comment'></div>柳河东尝言：「地虽胜，得人焉居之，则有增而高，有辟而广，有不待饰而已奂者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317987_comment'></div>盖惟胜流足以受胜槩欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317987_comment'></div>忆予前年冬直玉堂，君授简，而余以文书谢不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317987_comment'></div>居二年，并掌外制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317987_comment'></div>予方如沐漆求解，而君数数迫之不置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317987_comment'></div>方连上祠请，倘幸蒙恩还里，则将挟溪童畦丁，携茶鼎笔床，从君绿山间，可以翛然而赋矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1317987_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　又言程奎奸污事，皆取消任命。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　廷鸾兼同编国史、实录院同修撰。作品：辞免兼国史申省状。<div id='poem_1317857' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317857' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317857?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免兼国史申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1263年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317857")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317857_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317857'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317857'>史籍策勋，已有汗青之日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317857_comment'></div>除书假宠，旋增尸素之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317857_comment'></div>闻命自天，措躬无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317857_comment'></div>伏念某疏慵特甚，忝冒居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317857_comment'></div>百短具呈，三长安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317857_comment'></div>侍玉皇之案，已腼螭坳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317857_comment'></div>䌷金匮之书，曷充马走？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317857_comment'></div>曩尝庀职，未睹成劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317857_comment'></div>今值明时，促登大典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317857_comment'></div>授简何资于末至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317857_comment'></div>奏篇寖迫于上陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317857_comment'></div>空空索己而竭焉，岂独愧鄙夫之问？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317857_comment'></div>碌碌因人而成者，又徒惭下士之招。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317857_comment'></div>欲望公朝，特赐敷奏，收回误渥，俾服旧官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317857_comment'></div>言为尚书，姑谨殿庭之记；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317857_comment'></div>职在太史，免尘渠观之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317857_comment'></div>庶竭谫材，上酬洪造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317857_comment'></div>所有上件恩命，未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1317857_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　文天祥除尚书礼部员外郎，廷鸾草制，盛赞其正义骨梗。作品：《文天祥除尚书礼部员外郎制》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文天祥官礼部事，《宋史·文天祥传》不载，舒大刚《年谱》姑系于此年。）</span><div id='poem_1317687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文天祥除尚书礼部员外郎制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1263年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317687")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317687'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317687'>吾甚遴郎选，尤重儒科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317687_comment'></div>倘以抡魁为表，郎其庶矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317687_comment'></div>尔藻思清新，词华敏茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317687_comment'></div>荣进素定，匪徒诧于高名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317687_comment'></div>慷慨敢言，盖已观其初节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317687_comment'></div>擢从郡最，登之郎闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317687_comment'></div>夫立乎人之本朝，而培养器业以答扬光宠者，必有在矣，岂直百日掌纶言、十年至两制之谓乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317687_comment'></div>大车以载，务积厥中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317687_comment'></div>朱绂方来，以艾尔后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317687_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1317687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　长子端复当荫补，夫人张氏令推恩于兄子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　迁礼部侍郎。作品：除礼部侍郎谢上表、除礼侍谢马裕斋启。<div id='poem_1317848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除礼部侍郎谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317848")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317848'>王制禄，则赞书久尘内史；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317848_comment'></div>帝咨能，而典礼遽贰秩宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317848_comment'></div>带悸有容，衣华已泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317848_comment'></div>感深滋惧，恩厚难任<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317848_comment'></div>窃以侍从班穹，礼官责重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317848_comment'></div>韩愈奏薄技，自许文章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317848_comment'></div>叔孙召鄙儒，不通时变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317848_comment'></div>况复愧汉唐之士，若为事尧舜之君？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317848_comment'></div>伏念臣一介羁孤，千龄际遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317848_comment'></div>甘泉宫，玉堂殿，承诏才悭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317848_comment'></div>水苍佩，进贤冠，章身德薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317848_comment'></div>漫尘两制，初乏一长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317848_comment'></div>天章下饬于禁林，宠过令狐之夜炬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317848_comment'></div>海润无裨于储寀，讥同公干之春华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317848_comment'></div>维鹈不濡，瞻乌欲哺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317848_comment'></div>舍肉屡贻于颍谷，归耕独恋于绵田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317848_comment'></div>重污高绅，荐干閒廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317848_comment'></div>迟颁俞旨，早被恩言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317848_comment'></div>孰谓知礼乎，既惭绵蕝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317848_comment'></div>何以谓文也，仍绾丝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317848_comment'></div>伛躬腰下之黄金，腼面阶前之红药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317848_comment'></div>荣名过渥，窳器易盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317848_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下任官惟贤，知人则哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317848_comment'></div>惟天明畏，必惇典庸礼以代天工；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317848_comment'></div>作民孚先，必发号施令而达民说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317848_comment'></div>讵容驽蹇，叠冒宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317848_comment'></div>臣内揆所蒙，长怀未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317848_comment'></div>圣人为礼教，式敷降典之邦彝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317848_comment'></div>明主可忠言，敢愧进思之宸笔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1317848_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除礼侍谢马裕斋启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317873")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317873'>滥尘西掖，曾微视草之长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317873_comment'></div>擢贰南宫，遽冒为真之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317873_comment'></div>控辞未获，伛受奚胜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317873_comment'></div>惟伯夷三礼之咨，虞朝盛选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317873_comment'></div>若知章两命之拜，唐世美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317873_comment'></div>苟非其人，不在兹位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317873_comment'></div>伏念某学虽志道，才不逾人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317873_comment'></div>再登宏达之科，寖历清华之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317873_comment'></div>朝裾久缀，甚有愧于鹈濡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317873_comment'></div>祠廪屡干，莫少安于乌哺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317873_comment'></div>迟颁俞旨，早拜恩言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317873_comment'></div>孰谓知礼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317873_comment'></div>已惭绵蕝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317873_comment'></div>何以谓文也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317873_comment'></div>更绾丝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317873_comment'></div>退省其私，敢忘所自？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317873_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官，人才元气，王室股肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317873_comment'></div>念举尔所知，常入古灵荐士藁之目；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317873_comment'></div>况不如同姓，更深老泉《族谱引》之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317873_comment'></div>昔以此论道经邦，今以此开府作牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317873_comment'></div>遂使门生之下品，躐登禁路之清曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317873_comment'></div>眷私夙播于大钧，庆奖益勤于小物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317873_comment'></div>某敢不益坚素守，仰报殊知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317873_comment'></div>汝作秩宗，何补论思之列？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317873_comment'></div>帝赉良弼，亟膺图象之求。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1317873_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年4月</a>　四月，为皇太子生日作诗。作品：《皇太子生日诗》<div id='poem_56824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇太子生辰诗三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1262年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56824")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56824'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56824'>煌煌炎宋兴，奕世开燕谋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56824'>建隆圣人出，庚年宝运周。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56824'>祥符帝子生，巳月神光流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56824'>稽首颂储君，昭哉遹嘉猷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56824'>吹铜协乾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>阳，主鬯弥千秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56824'>星晖狼弧低，海润青齐收。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56824'>金轮整鹤驾，玉觞侍龙楼。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56824'>无逸能为<span class='inlineComment2'>（《诗渊》作惟能）</span>寿，乾乾谨时休<span class='inlineComment2'>（《诗渊》作脩　自注：壬戌。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56824'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_56824_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_56824'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_56824_0'>⑴ 《诗渊》册六页四四九一作六</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_56824_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_56823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56823?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1263年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56823'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56823'>苍龙见天东，房驷拱辰北。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56823'>煌煌心星前，炳炳天王侧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56823'>休符协乾文，正阳毓紫<span class='inlineComment2'>（《诗渊》作垂）</span>极。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56823'>铜楼蔼祥光，玉卮奉愉色。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56823'>叹声沸笙鸾，寿龄指箕翼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56823'>何以祝元良，勉哉崇明德。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56823'>学问日就将，福禄时万亿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56823'>永侍帝宸尊，重晖照四国<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：癸亥。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56823_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56823'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_56823_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56822?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年4月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_56822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56822'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56822'>正阳毓前星，盛事符仁祖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56822'>仁者寿之基，生意一何溥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56822'>欢愉侍宫庭，晖润弥海宇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56822'>三朝谨师文，寸阴勤惜禹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56822'>新功鉴铭盘，妙用明絜矩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_56822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_56822'>嘉宾从商园，末僚愧韩愈。<div id='poem_sentence_5_56822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_56822'>永言祝储君，重离日常午<span class='inlineComment2'>（《诗渊》句作英略如望父）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_56822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_56822'>八表跻春台，万年受天祜<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：甲子。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_56822_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_56822'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_56822_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　抗蒙英雄王坚致仕加恩，廷鸾拟制褒之。作品：《王坚致仕加恩制》<div id='poem_1317812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王坚致仕加恩制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317812")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317812'>门下：朕念边陲控带之邦，倚勋杰捍城之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317812_comment'></div>老当益壮，方图将军之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317812_comment'></div>归不待年，忽致大夫之仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317812_comment'></div>甫赖整师于淮浦，讵期谢病于频阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317812_comment'></div>莫遏雅怀，其敷异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317812_comment'></div>具官某，性根忠义，资禀沈雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317812_comment'></div>结发而战匈奴，彯缨而号飞将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317812_comment'></div>念昔铜梁之绩，重清玉垒之昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317812_comment'></div>冲梯舞云，莫夺墨家之守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317812_comment'></div>枯泉飞液，咸敬汉德之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317812_comment'></div>西师歌心胆之寒，北道裹糇粮而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317812_comment'></div>径登斋钺，来护周庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317812_comment'></div>乃眷历阳，实维钜镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317812_comment'></div>外峙边头之保障，内增江面之藩篱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317812_comment'></div>宜宣老熊当道之威，遽览神虎挂冠之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317812_comment'></div>昔盱眙奋剑，力全臧质之城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317812_comment'></div>今南郡赐金，孰愈吕蒙之疾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317812_comment'></div>何恙不已，鲜我方将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317812_comment'></div>仪辨三孤，乃参华于亚傅：爵冠五等，仍进列于群公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317812_comment'></div>并衍圭租，俾安药石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317812_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317812_comment'></div>听磬思封疆之烈，靡忘著令以称忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317812_comment'></div>悬车传子孙之荣，犹可阖门而养重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317812_comment'></div>尚其冲啬，对此褒庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317812_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1317812_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　夏，廷鸾迁礼部尚书。作品：除礼部尚书辞免奏状。<div id='poem_1317842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除权礼部尚书辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317842")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317842'>自天有命，无地措躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317842_comment'></div>切以文昌从列之最高，仪曹邦典之尤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317842_comment'></div>讵谓孤踪之宜去，乃逢显擢以摄承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317842_comment'></div>伏念臣被遇先皇，侥踰近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317842_comment'></div>徒以文辞之薄技，适遭明主之殊知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317842_comment'></div>武帝赐淮南王，祗愧平时之视草；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317842_comment'></div>成王命召太保，惊闻一旦之顾言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317842_comment'></div>万宇摧心，三灵变色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317842_comment'></div>恭际《大明》之出，收悲以欣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317842_comment'></div>幸逢《小毖》之求，举直错枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317842_comment'></div>此群材连茹之日，实寸草归根之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317842_comment'></div>惟先帝蜕衣冠而宾空，汗漫之游远矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317842_comment'></div>若微臣执笔墨而事主，进退之谊何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317842_comment'></div>莫获徇身，正宜屏迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317842_comment'></div>初非贪恋，尚希进于明时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317842_comment'></div>姑示从容，恐重伤于圣抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317842_comment'></div>胡为越躐，骤有跻攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317842_comment'></div>欲望皇帝陛下，洞达圣聪，俯矜愚悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317842_comment'></div>于此时而峻陟，沥血以辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317842_comment'></div>若异日之甄陶，捐躯而报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317842_comment'></div>所有上件恩命，臣未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1317842_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年6月</a>　六月，理宗御制诗赐廷鸾及牟子才，廷鸾作表谢，和其韵，将御诗刻石。作品：谢御赐诗表、进和御制诗表、恭和御制诗表。<div id='poem_1317846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢御赐诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317846")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317846'>臣有常宪，递直玉堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317846_comment'></div>帝庸作歌，骤颁宝画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317846_comment'></div>词林盛事，儒藻荣观<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317846_comment'></div>切以内禁申严，诸儒儤直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317846_comment'></div>八砖晚簉，未许倦游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317846_comment'></div>三伏早归，才容夙退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317846_comment'></div>率沿唐世，以暨本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317846_comment'></div>惟昭代之右文，于儒臣而假宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317846_comment'></div>凝酥入咏，昉常锡于宸章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317846_comment'></div>前席兴思，亿荷蒙于圣制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317846_comment'></div>至如易简，尤遇熙陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317846_comment'></div>彼皆杰然之才，宜被焕乎之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317846_comment'></div>如臣者，汲同短绠，吹类寒竽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317846_comment'></div>自惭操上水之舟，每念草归田之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317846_comment'></div>比由夜直，首沐天恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317846_comment'></div>郢醪初设于上方，闽荔仍颁于远物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317846_comment'></div>事光前代，眷迥异时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317846_comment'></div>未踰浃日之期，重拜非烟之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317846_comment'></div>身兼两制，滥陪从雍之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317846_comment'></div>运际千龄，骤捧横汾之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317846_comment'></div>恩由上出，感自中深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317846_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下睿藻日新，皇猷天纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317846_comment'></div>虞弦协奏，上同帝舜之乃文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317846_comment'></div>汉筑漫歌，俯陋高皇之未学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317846_comment'></div>奎画龙鸾之眩晃，天章河汉之昭回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317846_comment'></div>若稽淳化之初，绝出中兴之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317846_comment'></div>圣谟有炜，至德难名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317846_comment'></div>臣捧戴有荣，袭藏惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317846_comment'></div>写之琬琰，所宜续旧制于金坡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317846_comment'></div>传之子孙，常恐发神光于蔀屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317846_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣，激切屏营之至！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317846_comment'></div>景定五年六月某日，朝请大夫、试中书舍人、兼权直学士院、兼同编修国史、实录院同修撰、兼太子庶子臣某表。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1317846_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进和御制诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317847")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317847_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317847'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317847'>恭惟皇帝陛下睿谟浚发，圣藻彰施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317847_comment'></div>天纵又多能，侈龙鸾之妙画；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317847_comment'></div>帝光饬万物，掞河汉之宸章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317847_comment'></div>比词臣入直于金坡，乃御制亲颁于宝画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317847_comment'></div>焜煌圣作，黼黻儒流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317847_comment'></div>赐龙笺之题，淳化初褒于易简；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317847_comment'></div>揭玉堂之榜，绍兴重锡于麟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317847_comment'></div>兹兴起于人文，亦对扬于祖武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317847_comment'></div>臣谬充鳌禁，叨被龙光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317847_comment'></div>羞薄技之前陈，持庸音而赓载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317847_comment'></div>大明委照，爝火安敢以呈辉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317847_comment'></div>迅霆发声，众籁自为之息响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317847_comment'></div>退循荒斐，弥积兢惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317847_comment'></div>谨恭和成二首，上渎圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317847_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1317847_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年夏</a>　建从官宅、进思堂，理宗题额，廷鸾作记。作品：《恭题从官宅进思堂宸翰》<div id='poem_1317905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恭题从官宅进思堂宸翰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317905")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317905'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317905'>恭惟国家驻跸吴会，东南旗盖，应运中兴，太紫圆方，侔天作制，承平百年，官府寺第，固已粲乎，隐隐各得其所矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317905_comment'></div>爰自绍兴，给降御前钱，造府以居执政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317905_comment'></div>乾道辟怀远驿基，以处台谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317905_comment'></div>而从臣官舍，未有攸居，国史无述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317905_comment'></div>景定四年秋，从官宅始成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317905_comment'></div>其明年夏，权礼部尚书臣某言：「臣待罪春官，幸得与诸臣割宅而居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317905_comment'></div>则又为之规隙地，筑室三楹，欲于自公退食之际，修进思尽忠之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317905_comment'></div>臣敢昧死请『进思堂』三大字，示臣子伫瞻，秉心宣猷，永照无极」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317905_comment'></div>奏函朝入，天笔夕颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317905_comment'></div>奎章圣藻，日月并明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317905_comment'></div>璇榜云楣，丹雘无色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317905_comment'></div>诸臣拜手稽首，仰瞻神文，相与言曰：思之义大矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317905_comment'></div>皋陶、禹之在虞廷也，其赞赞日思，其孜孜日思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317905_comment'></div>周公兼三王，施四事，孟子两以思言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317905_comment'></div>荀林父，霸国之臣也，其进思尽忠，则仲尼取而列之经，以为万世臣子事君之大训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317905_comment'></div>凡士自一命以上，莫不职思其忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317905_comment'></div>而侍从者，论思献纳之臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317905_comment'></div>先正司马温国文正公光，因辞副枢，论国事，而曰：「臣于未受命，则犹从臣也，于事无所不可言者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317905_comment'></div>古之为从臣，盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317905_comment'></div>彼有便文自营，而谓君子思不出位者，偷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317905_comment'></div>玩岁愒时，而谓天下何思何虑者，妄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317905_comment'></div>若夫「憧憧往来，朋从尔思」，而所营不过乎患得患失之间，则其于为人贤不肖何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317905_comment'></div>《诗》曰「倬彼云汉，为章于天」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317905_comment'></div>渊哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317905_comment'></div>尧文丕天之大律也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317905_comment'></div>又曰：「上帝临汝，无贰尔心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317905_comment'></div>论思之臣，其勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317905_comment'></div>臣等谨奉宸翰，刻之琬琰，因并著其语于下方，以风示同列云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317905_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年7月</a>　七月，彗星出，上书言天人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年10月</a>　十月，理宗崩，度宗即位，廷鸾草诏，并作贺登极表。作品：《景定五年十月丁卯诏》（代理宗）、《求言诏》（代度宗）、《贺皇帝登寳位表》<div id='poem_1317629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317629' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317629?labeling=true' target='_blank'>景定五年十月丁卯诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317629")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317629_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317629'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317629'>朕嗣守基图，君临区宇，历四十一年，内揆菲凉，罔敢暇逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317629_comment'></div>荷高穹之眷命，蒙列圣之遗休，洪济艰难，图惟康乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317629_comment'></div>岁事荐登，而民生厎定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317629_comment'></div>沴气即弭，而边尘寖清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317629_comment'></div>朕方益勉修攘，居怀儆戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317629_comment'></div>积勤爽豫，有加无瘳，乃至大渐，恐不得负扆见群臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317629_comment'></div>皇太子温文夙著，仁孝有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317629_comment'></div>升储副者五年，久参裁于庶务，宜自春宫而嗣服，允符至道之旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317629_comment'></div>可于柩前即皇帝位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317629_comment'></div>皇后佐佑朕躬，章明坤载，可尊为皇太后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317629_comment'></div>应军国事务，并听皇帝处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317629_comment'></div>尔其式遵成宪，诞受多方，益奉母仪，恪遵慈训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317629_comment'></div>皇帝成服，三日听政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317629_comment'></div>丧纪以日易月，群臣共为宽释，勿过摧伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317629_comment'></div>百官入临，并随地之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317629_comment'></div>诸道州府长吏以下，三日释服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317629_comment'></div>在京禁音乐百日，在外一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317629_comment'></div>无禁祀祠嫁娶，缘边不用举哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317629_comment'></div>山陵制度，务从俭约，应中外诸军支赐及其他不在诏中者，并听皇帝处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317629_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317629_comment'></div>人羡久生，奈盈虚之有数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317629_comment'></div>天惟纯佑，繄付托之得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317629_comment'></div>更赖股肱之元臣，文武列辟，交修不逮，协赞丕平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317629_comment'></div>咨尔群伦，体予至意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1317629_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求言诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317630")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317630'>朕荷列圣之储休，膺先皇之传祚，顾惟菲质，获缵丕图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317630_comment'></div>烛理昧而何以周知群情，更事浅而何以裁成庶务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317630_comment'></div>继犹判涣，其如多难之未堪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317630_comment'></div>不遑康宁，永惟万事之有阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317630_comment'></div>肆初临听，合广咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317630_comment'></div>天难忱斯，孰为迓续之本？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317630_comment'></div>民亦劳止，孰为绥靖之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317630_comment'></div>上而朕躬之愆违，次而朝政之得失，外则边陲之利害，下而田里之戚休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317630_comment'></div>惟言路之宏开，为新政之急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317630_comment'></div>用求忠谠，期厎敉宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317630_comment'></div>若昔大猷，盖有辟门之典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317630_comment'></div>闵予小子，敢忘谋庙之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317630_comment'></div>言而可行，则匪徒容纳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317630_comment'></div>试之既效，则宜示宠嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317630_comment'></div>悉意以陈，尔无悼于后害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317630_comment'></div>虚心而听，朕方伫于嘉谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317630_comment'></div>咨尔多方，体予至意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1317630_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1317853' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317853' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317853?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺皇帝登宝位表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317853")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317853_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317853'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317853'>统接千岁，王者无私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317853_comment'></div>明照四方，大人有继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317853_comment'></div>华夷胥悦，宇宙一新<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317853_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下神授英奇，性钟睿哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317853_comment'></div>圣功养正，期于传不勤而师不烦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317853_comment'></div>帝位履中，必也天助顺而人助信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317853_comment'></div>讴歌有属，历数攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317853_comment'></div>遵圣父之顾言，敬保元子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317853_comment'></div>奉太皇之慈训，拥佑神孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317853_comment'></div>稽《春秋》立嫡之文，法《大易》体元之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317853_comment'></div>一人有庆，天下为公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317853_comment'></div>臣荷朝厚恩，忝国旧辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317853_comment'></div>河清海宴，共欣圣作之辰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317853_comment'></div>山高日升，快睹时平之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317853_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1317853_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　廷鸾以太子府故人，转四官。作品：随龙转四官辞免奏状。<div id='poem_1317841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>随龙转四官辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定五年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317841")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317841'>鹤禁执经，漫尘攀附；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317841_comment'></div>龙飞赐秩，特愧超踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317841_comment'></div>躐等既深，循墙敢后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317841_comment'></div>伏念臣素持朴学，恭际盛时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317841_comment'></div>三年获侍于承华，一得何裨于新益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317841_comment'></div>性能天授，本由圣学之高明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317841_comment'></div>日就月将，安取愚臣之辅翼？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317841_comment'></div>然且每盈岁籥，辄被宸纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317841_comment'></div>兹继照于离明，复诞扬于涣汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317841_comment'></div>不遗故旧，丕昭伐木之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317841_comment'></div>若假器名，徒重繁缨之锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317841_comment'></div>恭望皇帝陛下俯怜卑悃，亟寝误恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317841_comment'></div>傅不勤，师不烦，昔已大成于后德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317841_comment'></div>官不谄，士不滥，今宜益肃于朝纲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1317841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　度宗即位，赐理宗朝故老，廷鸾草诏。作品：《赐先朝故老大臣诏》<div id='poem_1317632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317632?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐先朝故老大臣诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317632")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317632_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317632'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317632'>朕纂承先帝之丕图，注想朝廷之故老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317632_comment'></div>天下大器，念付托之惟艰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317632_comment'></div>旧德元龟，方咨诹之是急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317632_comment'></div>眷言勋辅，式燕殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317632_comment'></div>曩属时艰，屡膺事柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317632_comment'></div>入则谋谟廊庙，出则控驭边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317632_comment'></div>中国四夷，每想闻其风采；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317632_comment'></div>元侯宿将，尝禀听其指呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317632_comment'></div>岂惟朝廷之周知，盖亦帷筹之熟讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317632_comment'></div>凡修攘之大政，有老成之远谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317632_comment'></div>惟天全付予有家，欲恢先绪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317632_comment'></div>乃心罔不在王室，宜罄忠猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317632_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1317632_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　又赐侍读、侍讲诸人，廷鸾草诏。作品：《赐侍读侍讲说书官诏》<div id='poem_1317631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐侍读侍讲说书官诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317631")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317631'>朕以菲质，夙承义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317631_comment'></div>先皇帝贻厥孙谋，莫详资善之一记；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317631_comment'></div>予小子兹迪彝教，俾亲博雅之群儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317631_comment'></div>勉奉遗谟，初承大统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317631_comment'></div>感畴昔之问安视膳，予惟见于墙、见于羹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317631_comment'></div>矧今日之发政施仁，且欲观其志、观其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317631_comment'></div>傥非讲学，何以绍图？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317631_comment'></div>王人求多闻，必精研于古训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317631_comment'></div>天下治在道，宜深究于理源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317631_comment'></div>惟对贤士大夫之时常多，则于古先帝王之道有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317631_comment'></div>由尧舜禹汤而汲汲，犹恐失之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317631_comment'></div>论唐虞仁圣以䜣䜣，我自乐此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317631_comment'></div>肆因初服，首辟经帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317631_comment'></div>既登进于旧游，且旁延于时望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317631_comment'></div>惟端平亲政，读《衍义》之成书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317631_comment'></div>惟景祐盛时，陈正说之丕训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317631_comment'></div>稽累朝谟烈之懿，暨七篇仁义之陈，六经之道与同归，百世俟圣而不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317631_comment'></div>自求自趣，开予以厌饫优柔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317631_comment'></div>所知所行，迪我于高明光大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317631_comment'></div>锐期磋切，周广缉熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317631_comment'></div>庶君德之日强，则治功之益进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317631_comment'></div>予其自勉，尔尚交修。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1317631_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年10月30日</a>　大赦天下，廷鸾草首尾词。作品：《皇帝登宝位赦文首尾词》<div id='poem_1317667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝登宝位赦文首尾词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年10月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317667")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317667'>门下：帝王统群生，实任抚绥之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317667_comment'></div>《春秋》正五始，况承付托之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317667_comment'></div>仰惟先皇，丕昭前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317667_comment'></div>继序十有三圣，光绍宁宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317667_comment'></div>享国四十一年，远几仁祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317667_comment'></div>视民若保，事帝如临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317667_comment'></div>以江海之量，优容群言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317667_comment'></div>以雨露之恩，渗漉九有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317667_comment'></div>时和屡格，敌难坐消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317667_comment'></div>日引月长，久于其道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317667_comment'></div>蚤朝晏罢，遹求厥宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317667_comment'></div>圣躬莫惮于焦劳，冲候遂愆于节适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317667_comment'></div>兴言菲质，恭侍宸庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317667_comment'></div>解带靡遑，所期日间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317667_comment'></div>抱弓何及，讵意天摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317667_comment'></div>惊闻凭几之言，俾奉缵图之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317667_comment'></div>恪承慈极，勤抚多方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317667_comment'></div>创钜痛深，且嬛嬛而在疚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317667_comment'></div>投艰遗大，尤栗栗以弗胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317667_comment'></div>惟天地之德好生，惟祖宗以仁立国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317667_comment'></div>矧属君临之初政，式循覃沛之旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317667_comment'></div>可大赦天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317667_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317667_comment'></div>天付有家传在予，必稽谋而疾敬德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317667_comment'></div>父有天下归于子，惟永念而弗弃基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317667_comment'></div>庶能慰六军万姓之同心，于以答中国四夷之望治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317667_comment'></div>尚赖忠贤硕辅、文武具僚，协济康功，共扶休运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317667_comment'></div>布告中外，咸使闻知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317667_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　度宗初听政，廷鸾、留梦炎并兼侍读，既而廷鸾升直学士院。作品：兼侍读辞免奏状。<div id='poem_1317843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兼侍读辞免奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317843")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317843'>自天有命，蹐地无容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317843_comment'></div>伏念臣学殖空荒，见闻单浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317843_comment'></div>比充员于新益，获侍龙潜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317843_comment'></div>蔑有补于就将，漫随鸿翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317843_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下，体乾刚健，位履正中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317843_comment'></div>《大明》方升，正懋缉熙之学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317843_comment'></div>《小毖》求助，尤资访问之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317843_comment'></div>嗣德在初，知人则哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317843_comment'></div>欲讲明于毡厦，宜简拔于髦英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317843_comment'></div>非道不陈，必有孟轲之素学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317843_comment'></div>唯材是与，难私秦府之旧僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317843_comment'></div>欲望皇帝陛下深轸圣慈，俯矜愚悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317843_comment'></div>特收成命，宜亟畀于名流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317843_comment'></div>俾阐大猷，以上培于新德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317843_comment'></div>所有上件恩命，臣未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1317843_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　十二月，廷鸾进讲《大学衍义序》，陈“心法”之要。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e87df75298ed4d86972bf4ceccee7117_label'><a href='javascript:
