ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年闰五月16日</a>　闰五月，癸丑，江万里为参知政事，廷鸾作贺启。作品：《贺江参政启》<div id='poem_1317875' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317875' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317875?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺江参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1265年闰五月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317875")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317875_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317875'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317875'>显奉明纶，荣参大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317875_comment'></div>人惟求旧，上方坚图任之忱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317875_comment'></div>民具尔瞻，公厚积登庸之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317875_comment'></div>邮传闿怿，庙论崇谹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317875_comment'></div>恭惟某官一代宗工，两朝旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317875_comment'></div>澄不清，淆不浊，直哉惟清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317875_comment'></div>用弥壮，宿弥明，美之谓大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317875_comment'></div>曩追先帝之殊遇，来翊圣主之初元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317875_comment'></div>卷舒不随乎时，进退必以其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317875_comment'></div>青山逸兴，方开洛下之书堂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317875_comment'></div>白纻好词，催牧江东之要郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317875_comment'></div>适期年之报政，会霖雨之思贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317875_comment'></div>以我公归兮，大慰仪刑之注想；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317875_comment'></div>有为王言者，式观仁义之敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317875_comment'></div>某又获抠趋，夙欣缘缔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317875_comment'></div>为晋公护中书印，宜谨视于银黄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317875_comment'></div>效眉山赋《内前行》，愧不工于笔墨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1317875_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年</a>　除端明殿学士、签书枢密院事,、兼同提举编修《经武要略》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年</a>　母段氏封太夫人。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='134549caf4be4c56a03e06425fe929a2_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年12月26日</a>　十二月，理宗袝庙，廷鸾拟辞。作品：《烈文仁武圣明孝皇帝袝庙德音》<div id='poem_1317668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>烈文仁武圣明安孝皇帝祔庙德音</a><span class='authorDate'>（1266年12月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317668")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317668'>门下：朕永言孝思，以当大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317668_comment'></div>于乎皇考，维继序之不忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317668_comment'></div>瞻彼昊天，欲酬恩而罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317668_comment'></div>丧饰三年之纪，葬遵七月之彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317668_comment'></div>龟筮告期，龙㡛即路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317668_comment'></div>天维显相，胥江之波涛不兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317668_comment'></div>民靡告劳，会稽之人徒毕集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317668_comment'></div>甫临真域，式迄羡封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317668_comment'></div>八翣五重，必诚必信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317668_comment'></div>千秋万岁，既固既安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317668_comment'></div>吉仗回虞，新宫登祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317668_comment'></div>嗟嬛嬛在疚之日，赖蹇蹇匪躬之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317668_comment'></div>三公在朝，力请廞仪之办护；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317668_comment'></div>百官承事，咸遵命戒之驱驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317668_comment'></div>念虽循俭约之训言，顾宁免绎骚之烦费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317668_comment'></div>菆涂载启，京师同陟岵之悲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317668_comment'></div>窀穸孔严，近辅奉因山之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317668_comment'></div>输勤惟谨，趋事敢稽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317668_comment'></div>井赋缧囚，悉从宽宥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317668_comment'></div>岳祇渎祀，咸与封崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317668_comment'></div>亟敷汤网之宽，少慰尧墙之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317668_comment'></div>时为旧典，匪我私恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317668_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317668_comment'></div>唐宗葬近桥陵，未忘孝敬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317668_comment'></div>汉帝魂思沛邑，尚议复除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317668_comment'></div>知予仰体于遗仁，咨尔具敷于德意。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年</a>　服阕，回朝，知贡举，王应麟权直。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年</a>　度宗皇帝赐新进士诗，廷鸾和之。作品：《恭和御制进士韵》<div id='poem_56761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年8月</a>　除同知枢密院事，兼提举编修《经武要略》作品：提举官进上经武要略。<div id='poem_1317851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>提举官进上经武要略表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317851")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317851'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317851'>于昭皇武，续唐雅之献歌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317851_comment'></div>有赫神谟，轶《汉书》之辑略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317851_comment'></div>吉涓谷旦，肃上瑶编<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317851_comment'></div>伏以国家紫盖黄旗，上应东南之运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317851_comment'></div>金城铁壁，外严西北之防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317851_comment'></div>彻桑常谨于绸缪，汗竹不胜其纪载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317851_comment'></div>武有七德，务保大以为先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317851_comment'></div>天生五材，欲去兵而不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317851_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下乾旋坤转，日照月临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317851_comment'></div>登瀚海，铭燕然，蚤欲挽尚文之弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317851_comment'></div>赋《采薇》，歌《杕杜》，永无忘经武之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317851_comment'></div>诘尔戎兵，戒我师旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317851_comment'></div>惟中兴五世之业，丕显丕承；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317851_comment'></div>自淳祐四祀以来，且攻且守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317851_comment'></div>爪士持弓而御塞，元臣授钺以临边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317851_comment'></div>北复襄樊，南通交广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317851_comment'></div>候望不撤乎四境，筹帷每出于万全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317851_comment'></div>马饮江湖，坐送佛狸之死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317851_comment'></div>兵传风鹤，遄驱草付之亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317851_comment'></div>既侈伐功，爰修武志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317851_comment'></div>混夷駾矣，聿昭御侮之良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317851_comment'></div>皇王烝哉，丕播骏声之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317851_comment'></div>视诸故府，钦乃攸司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317851_comment'></div>裁为百卷之奏篇，必提其要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317851_comment'></div>载缵九年之行事，皆聚此书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317851_comment'></div>臣等莫补宏纲，愿规常德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317851_comment'></div>春秋无义战，于二三策以何称？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317851_comment'></div>帝王有要经，斯十一征而无敌。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1317851_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年</a>　入奏，以重本、宽大、仁厚为言。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_1317633_comment'></div>眷言淮左，有若滁阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317633_comment'></div>自五代之际，迄百年以来，虽人民城郭之或非，尚陵阿泉池之不改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317633_comment'></div>艺祖肇基王迹，所纪戎功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317633_comment'></div>先皇敷遗后人，欲固吾国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317633_comment'></div>有嘉阃制，能体庙谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317633_comment'></div>百堵皆兴，不愆于素；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317633_comment'></div>五月而毕，迄溃于成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317633_comment'></div>比峻壑之凭陵，望崇墉而却走。<div class='inline' href='/Writing/1317850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同知枢密院事兼参政谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1268年4月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317850'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317850'>召节载驰，促朝魏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317850_comment'></div>恩书狎被，擢贰机庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317850_comment'></div>恍惊诏綍之新荣，躐进筹帷之故步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317850_comment'></div>仰瞻天咫，俯切冰兢<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317850_comment'></div>伏以国之大事在戎，况关兵本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317850_comment'></div>王任旧人共政，实倚贤谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317850_comment'></div>茍非其人，不在此位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317850_comment'></div>伏念臣材惭庸琐，运际休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317850_comment'></div>两禁代言，有感贞元之朝士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317850_comment'></div>六龙御极，首登秦府之旧僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317850_comment'></div>而臣罂缶量盈，杯棬泽殄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317850_comment'></div>三年罹棘，已误太行之云飞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317850_comment'></div>一旦涂芝，又报长安之日近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317850_comment'></div>荷圣主记怜于中野徬徨之后，感公朝拔擢于穷山寂寞之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317850_comment'></div>与之琴而使弹，未忘切切；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317850_comment'></div>招以旌而欲往，宁独迟迟？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317850_comment'></div>已稽俟驾之诛，更被出纶之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317850_comment'></div>昔参宥命，今副事枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317850_comment'></div>藩臣勉谕于里闾，貂使传宣于畿辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317850_comment'></div>玉阶布武，方趋紫殿以称觞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317850_comment'></div>奎画陟明，复践黄扉而预政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317850_comment'></div>股肱所寄，踵顶莫酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317850_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下舜哲知人，尧仁遍物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317850_comment'></div>元祐之开皇极，既资彦博之壮猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317850_comment'></div>庆历之对天章，必擢仲淹之宿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317850_comment'></div>英辟丕承于祖武，孱儒曷继于前修？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317850_comment'></div>臣敢不仰戴洪休，自鞭驽钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317850_comment'></div>集思广益，无能效智于庙谟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317850_comment'></div>同寅协恭，惟知纯意于国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317850_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1317850_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年</a>　曹泾进士及第，廷鸾曾召置西席，以教端临兄弟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年8月</a>　八月，以奉安《宁宗实录》等书，廷鸾等各转两官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年2月</a>　正月，叶梦得进少保，廷鸾作贺启。作品：贺叶丞相少保启、回叶少保启、<div id='poem_1317881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺叶丞相除少保启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317881")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317881'>诞布廷麻，晋升班棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317881_comment'></div>总群书，奏七略，惟暨乃僚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317881_comment'></div>立少保，曰三孤，叙进其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317881_comment'></div>绅緌欢忭，廊庙尊崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317881_comment'></div>恭惟某官道蕴夔、龙，学卑迁、固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317881_comment'></div>兼三王，施四事，慨想前猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317881_comment'></div>黜百家，章六经，光辅明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317881_comment'></div>用铺张于谟烈，宜对越于宠灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317881_comment'></div>某获佐下风，欣逢盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317881_comment'></div>奋庸熙载而宅百揆，茂鬯斯文；<div class='inline' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317882?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回叶少保启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317882")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317882'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317882'>成国疏封，殊庭领使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317882_comment'></div>十连为帅，既力避于青油；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317882_comment'></div>三寿作朋，喜独颐于绿野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317882_comment'></div>搢绅叹仰，邮置欢传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317882_comment'></div>恭惟某官高节全名，钜人长德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317882_comment'></div>疏而霖雨，触石之云为兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317882_comment'></div>静乎深渊，出山之泉不浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317882_comment'></div>收功夔、契，抗志巢、由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317882_comment'></div>正是国人，胙之名壤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317882_comment'></div>保兹天子，秉乃桓圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317882_comment'></div>兹为平地之神仙，不碍山中之宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317882_comment'></div>某执鞭有志，贺厦无从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317882_comment'></div>黄閤紫枢，所愧滥巾之及我；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317882_comment'></div>青山流水，何时扶杖以从公？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317882_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1317882_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年正月18日</a>　参知政事兼同知枢密院事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年3月23日</a>　三月戊辰，除右丞相兼枢密使，江万里左丞相，与贾似道并相。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年</a>　陈文龙状元及第，为文谢廷鸾，作回书。作品：《答陈状元启》<div id='poem_1317872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答陈状元<span class='inlineComment2'>（文龙）</span>启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317872")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317872'>龙飞亲策，胪唱首登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317872_comment'></div>下明诏，发德音，大人造也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317872_comment'></div>字灵均，名正则，君子宜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317872_comment'></div>伏惟某官孕秀七闽，蜚英六馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317872_comment'></div>诵《上林》之伟作，相如最其善鸣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317872_comment'></div>得广川之醇儒，仲舒褎然举首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317872_comment'></div>声传寰海，欢动贤关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317872_comment'></div>盛事占五色云，修程破万里浪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317872_comment'></div>某比肩迩列，拭目奏篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317872_comment'></div>胡辱谦撝，过勤巽谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317872_comment'></div>发策决科，先天下事，已收盖世之鸿名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317872_comment'></div>犯颜敢谏，古大臣风，好续传家之相谱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317872_comment'></div>略陈赞颂，幸冀鉴融。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1317872_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年4月6日</a>　四月，辞免右相，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年2月</a>　正月，李庭芝为京湖路安抚制置使，李作谢书，廷鸾作答书。作品：回荆阃李端明庭芝启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年</a>　右丞相，与贾似道并。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年6月</a>　六月，贾似道托疾辞退，自马廷鸾以下部司，上书留之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年10月</a>　十月，理宗忌日，作诗。作品：《十月二十六日有感》<div id='poem_56788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>十月二十六日有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1270年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56788")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_56788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56788'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56788'>宾空后甲再经壬，香断金炉已七春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56788'>四十一年民父母，谁知今日帝乘云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56788'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　右丞相，与贾似道并。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　贾似道一日招马廷鸾、陆梦鼎饮，行令，举一物与人，还诗一联。似道云：“我有一局棋，付与棋师，棋师得之，予我一联诗：自出洞来无敌手，得饶人处且饶人。”廷鸾云：“我有一竿竹，付与渔翁，渔翁得之，予我一联诗：夜静水寒鱼不饵，满船空载月明归。”梦鼎云：“我有一张犁，付与农夫，农夫得之，予我一联诗：但存方寸地，留与子孙耕。”似道不悦而罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　汪泰轩廷对，不称旨，复上书万言，访廷鸾，遂起其辞相之念。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　廷鸾以疾辞相，出居六和塔，待命六十余日。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='417ad1018a4644089cf9be08dd20fcb7_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　任右丞相。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年10月</a>　十月，廷鸾十疏乞骸骨，诏不允。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年11月1日</a>　廷鸾扼于贾似道，力辞相位，乃以观文殿大学士知饶州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　廷鸾陛辞，深以时局为忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年11月5日</a>　己未，辞知饶州，乞祠禄，诏允所请，以观文殿大学士、鄱阳郡公提举洞霄宫。作品：谢除观文殿大学士提举临安府洞霄宫表。<div id='poem_1317852' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317852' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317852?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除观文殿大学士提举临安府洞霄宫表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年11月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317852")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317852_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317852'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317852'>相印上还，愧股肱之已隳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317852_comment'></div>宸纶中出，知体貌之未衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317852_comment'></div>侯藩许避于乡邦，书殿仍兼于祠廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317852_comment'></div>恩与天而同大，感无地以寄言<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317852_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以謏儒，获逢休运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317852_comment'></div>旁招俊乂，滥陪鸿翼之后尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317852_comment'></div>利见大人，亲睹龙飞之盛际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317852_comment'></div>粤从初政，已躐近班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317852_comment'></div>千秋无阀阅功，胡为取相？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317852_comment'></div>公孙有狗马病，宜亟避贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317852_comment'></div>惟其未尝施横草之劳，是以久而负积薪之困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317852_comment'></div>公朝宽大，假告频数而并容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317852_comment'></div>明主矜存，宣问稠重而不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317852_comment'></div>而臣任踰其分，福过于灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317852_comment'></div>不胜惟疾之忧，终冀乞身而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317852_comment'></div>叠干宸听，迄荷天从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317852_comment'></div>锡秘殿之穹班，予便藩于本郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317852_comment'></div>尚方薰茗以厚其宠，御府金币以华其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317852_comment'></div>终然徇伛偻之私，展也赋支离之粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317852_comment'></div>恭惟大造，绝出常伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317852_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下仁深善贷，德本好生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317852_comment'></div>念其景迫崦嵫，尚忧盈满；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317852_comment'></div>怜其身填沟壑，将遂宜休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317852_comment'></div>姑无意于荣名，俾自侪于旧弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317852_comment'></div>宠绥若此，报称谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317852_comment'></div>臣曷策枯羸，仰酬高厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317852_comment'></div>冢宰掌邦治，既蔑效于涓埃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317852_comment'></div>华封祝圣人，当力勤于香火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317852_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1317852_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　书其先人《课历序》后，发奋读书，凡经史子集，皆所拟读。作品：书课历序后。<div id='poem_1317936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书课历序后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317936")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317936'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317936'>右，先卫公馆北庄许氏时，课学者之遗训也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317936_comment'></div>可以课人，独不可以课其子孙乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317936_comment'></div>余家九男子，皆先公孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317936_comment'></div>余欲以先训课之，当自余自课始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317936_comment'></div>客曰：「汝以科举时文，适有天幸，试南宫，中首选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317936_comment'></div>入校中秘书，以至承华执经，露门劝讲，掌内外制，极朝廷文章翰墨之选，遂阶柄用，书不负汝，而汝负书多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317936_comment'></div>今年踰五十，饰巾待终而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317936_comment'></div>政使记三箧、读五车，渠能复于书有所发明乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317936_comment'></div>余曰：不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317936_comment'></div>杜祁公既致仕还家，年已七十，始学草书，即工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317936_comment'></div>苏黄门云：「人生逐日，胸次须出一好议论，若饱食暖衣，惟利欲是念，何以自别于禽兽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317936_comment'></div>余归蜀当杜门著书，不令废日」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317936_comment'></div>黄山谷云：「诸儿渐长，不可不加意教训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317936_comment'></div>人生家计，厚薄自系时命，但不可令断读书种子耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317936_comment'></div>然则，读书课子，愈老愈勤可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317936_comment'></div>余之自课，欲取六经从头䌷绎，编纂一番，自义疏以及诸家之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317936_comment'></div>今读《易》始尽六十四卦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317936_comment'></div>自《书》以往，皆当次第读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317936_comment'></div>尝取温公《通鉴》、张氏《指掌》，编纂《读史讨》，以至前朝，未成书，将嗣抄之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317936_comment'></div>读诸家文集，纂其英华，为《秘密藏》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317936_comment'></div>凡经史百氏，嘉言善行，有会于余心者，拟小东莱公《读书记》，为会心自览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317936_comment'></div>凡诸史已点校者，欲再读；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317936_comment'></div>凡诗章自陶、杜而下，以尽本朝诸名人之作，皆欲细读，以助晚年吟咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317936_comment'></div>倘天假之年，其所读当不止此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317936_comment'></div>今条其目于此编，岁计而月校之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317936_comment'></div>九子者，人付一编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317936_comment'></div>长而能自读者，取其心之所好者自读之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317936_comment'></div>幼而未能读者，吾授以所当读，禀于明师而读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317936_comment'></div>亦条其目于此编，岁计而月校之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317936_comment'></div>如先公遗训，且并著所为时文之业焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317936_comment'></div>既授此编之后，暇日，当有以语我来。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1317936_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　端临以荫补承事郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　书其先人《课历序》后，发奋读书，凡经史子集，皆所拟读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年春</a>　建归艇小斋，归卧其中。作品：癸酉春暮锺信甫寄诗次其韵。<div id='poem_56821' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56821' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_56821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56821'>舍生只惧本心失，犯患谁知尊足存。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56821_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='authorDate'>（1273年春）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56744_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56744'><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　端临兄弟应试，廷鸾作诗励之。作品：《二子就试》<div id='poem_56696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二儿就试</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56696")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_56696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56696'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56696'>老病吾今业已衰，已还魏笏尚支颐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56696'>祝儿指日传金榜，怀我当年别玉墀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56696'>殿陛详延方吁俊，江湖空旷剧忧时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_56696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_56696'>此行蹇谔论邦国，莫为区区杏苑诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_56696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_56696'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_56696_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　端临漕试第一。以父辞相位，未试京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年12月</a>　十二月，除知绍兴府，辞，提举临安府洞霄宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　归十日，兄岩甫卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　作祭亡兄文。作品：《祭亡兄提幹文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　为曾空青文集作序。作品：曾空青文集序。<div id='poem_1317895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曾空青文集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317895")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317895'>余尝诵涪翁「扶藜对藓」之吟、曲阜「把卷临灯」之句，固已心焉窃慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317895_comment'></div>曾公才章之盛，顾前修日远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317895_comment'></div>自乾、淳诸老，文字已多遗落，况过江前后间乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317895_comment'></div>然心向往之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317895_comment'></div>一日西堂吴太史为言：「此吾乡空青公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317895_comment'></div>有集藏于家」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317895_comment'></div>余方谋传抄，而公之诸孙、今广德郡侯、太博公寄余新刊集本，且徵言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317895_comment'></div>余惟曾氏自密国以儒学开迹，欧阳公称其「有德有言，足以上继点、参、元、西」，渊源所渐远矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317895_comment'></div>空青子弟起家，文章继世，潜逃于家尊柄用之时，缱绻于诸贤流落之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317895_comment'></div>中间灭迹毁庐，相随入党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317895_comment'></div>迨天地重开，迄能以三朝正论暴白之世，其视当时败国殄民、为魁为杰者之子孙补史咒神矫诬万世者，其贤不肖何如也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317895_comment'></div>昔石林叶公以「亲见扬雄」美其诗，以「新样元和」评其书，以「三风流」颂其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317895_comment'></div>近世李雁湖亦谓「人恶隽异，俗疵文雅」，如空青公，虽不偶于时，而文采烂然垂后著世者，不能掩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317895_comment'></div>空青，抚人，而葬于信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317895_comment'></div>断垣凄草，孤寄百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317895_comment'></div>太博监其州，始封崇表章之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317895_comment'></div>其遗文如鲁殿秦碑，见者珍惜，自可孤行于南丰、曲阜之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317895_comment'></div>斯举也，昭前文，孝也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317895_comment'></div>植遗绪，义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317895_comment'></div>今曾氏昆令季强，侍郎公以忠言嘉谟入从出藩，太博之为邦，以道得民，朝廷深知治行，将选表矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317895_comment'></div>其文章则集芳趾美，卓然一大家数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317895_comment'></div>江左诸王，所谓「未有七叶之中，爵位相继，人人有集如吾门」者，何足道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317895_comment'></div>何足道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317895_comment'></div>辄赞叹而书其后云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317895_comment'></div>癸酉某月某日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1317895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　西蜀费伯恭为子求婚于马氏，廷鸾以中女许焉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年5月</a>　五月，廷鸾辞免知绍兴，不允.夫人张氏以疾示使者，朝廷遂允所请。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年</a>　作诗，示程介夫。作品：《示程介夫》<div id='poem_56631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>示程介夫<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_56631")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_56631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56631'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56631'>流年何必共君参，九琐青山老一庵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56631'>试检乐天诗集看，明年半百又加三。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56631_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56631'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56631_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_56630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56630?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_56630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_56630'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_56630'>羊肠路险百千转，云梦胸吞八九宽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56630'>豆饭芋羹才足欲，水边林下即心安。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56630'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56630_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年8月1日</a>　八月，甲辰，下诏求言于江万里、叶梦鼎、马廷鸾等老臣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年8月18日</a>　廷鸾乞归田，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年11月</a>　廷鸾辞前任官，提举洞霄宫。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衢州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='06158d1a13514ee8aa57fc2d022ca3b2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("06158d1a13514ee8aa57fc2d022ca3b2");'><span id='06158d1a13514ee8aa57fc2d022ca3b2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>，27岁</div><div id='06158d1a13514ee8aa57fc2d022ca3b2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>　廷鸾及第后，与徐霖定交；廷试归，又访徐霖于衢州径畈。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
池州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='94b7227d8ff44746b634f78b28ba82a9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("94b7227d8ff44746b634f78b28ba82a9");'><span id='94b7227d8ff44746b634f78b28ba82a9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>，32岁</div><div id='94b7227d8ff44746b634f78b28ba82a9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　赴池州教授任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年2月1日</a>　在池阳。三省同奉圣旨，令赴都堂审察，辞不就。作品：《辞免召命申状》<div id='poem_1317854' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317854' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317854?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免召命申省状<span class='inlineComment2'>（时在池阳，召赴都堂审察。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317854")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317854_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317854'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317854'>伏准尚书省劄子，正月一日三省同奉圣旨，令赴都堂审察者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317854_comment'></div>伏念某穷乡下士，初无超异之才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317854_comment'></div>应举觅官，靡有廉退之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317854_comment'></div>为亲干禄，随群计偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317854_comment'></div>遭逢圣明，忝尘科第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317854_comment'></div>部授池阳教官，待次六年，甫就初任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317854_comment'></div>今者伏遇公朝，荐扬多士，必须资历稍深，然后召用未晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317854_comment'></div>至于堂审，合立外庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317854_comment'></div>若或贪恋恩荣，闻命奔走，伏恐下长士流躁竞之风，上累圣明综核之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317854_comment'></div>欲乞朝廷，且容某安意职业，讲求义理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317854_comment'></div>与一郡诸生，涵泳圣时教育之泽，以备使令于异日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317854_comment'></div>所有上件恩劄，未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1317854_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　朱熹曾孙朱濬尝从廷鸾学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　廷鸾在池州，以礼表率生徒。为县尉厅作记。作品：《池州贵池县尉厅记》<div id='poem_1317990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1317990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1317990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>池州贵池县尉厅记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1253年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", "poem_title_1317990")'>马廷鸾</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1317990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1317990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1317990'>出秀山门，可二百步，所得古闉阇之故址，隆然如伏龟，有官府翼乎其上者，贵池新尉廨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1317990_comment'></div>尉，秦官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1317990_comment'></div>由汉以来，凡掌武事者，皆得称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1317990_comment'></div>太尉至与丞相等尊，中尉巡徼京师，司隶督大奸猾，以至郡也、县也，莫不有尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1317990_comment'></div>尉于县为最卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1317990_comment'></div>官虽卑，其尊名自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1317990_comment'></div>今之仕者，顾不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1317990_comment'></div>贵池附于诸侯，尉出掾曹、参军下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1317990_comment'></div>旦朝，束带持手版趋尹，请诸所移檄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1317990_comment'></div>暮走田庐间，逐逐无停轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1317990_comment'></div>而桴鼓之警，发召之役，不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1317990_comment'></div>又俗吏尸厥官，伏如处女，茍幸终更，逝如脱兔，固无暇营所谓传舍者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1317990_comment'></div>以诿长官，长官讳钱怖粟，亦视陋忽倾而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1317990_comment'></div>先时，旧治台府，度为齐山书堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1317990_comment'></div>前尉徙治其旁军地，蘧篨一厦，不溃于成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1317990_comment'></div>寄迹僧庐，三徙而得今治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1317990_comment'></div>旁挹湖山，苍翠欲滴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1317990_comment'></div>下瞰闾阎，错绣如画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1317990_comment'></div>其规模促狭，而负踞高爽，犹之以卑官受尊名者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1317990_comment'></div>营之者，少仙杨君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1317990_comment'></div>赋之缗钱、斛米、木章、竹个者，明府郑君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1317990_comment'></div>杨君谓：「吾幸满三岁，且去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1317990_comment'></div>去而以遗所不知何人，若非斲山骨，书片辞，无以识永久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1317990_comment'></div>且望来者之茍能充之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1317990_comment'></div>子为我书所以」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1317990_comment'></div>余羞非文章家，独忆李太白《赠秋浦柳少府》之句，「一日乘小车，访君梅市边」，诵以美君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1317990_comment'></div>稍槩括而为之歌曰：「美轮奂兮翚飞，嗟不日兮成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1317990_comment'></div>旧萧索兮忽芳菲，望白云兮当翠微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1317990_comment'></div>闾阎静兮，人吏稀兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1317990_comment'></div>刀闲闲兮，犬鸡护篱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1317990_comment'></div>少仙之去兮，万里清辉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1317990_comment'></div>歌曲正酣，君诣大府，受约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1317990_comment'></div>余亦上马去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1317990_comment'></div>君名颖，字茂实，武夷文公之几世孙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1317990_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

彭泽

-----title
临安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0e23f6c6287a46b486cd1f8d92b06cab_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0e23f6c6287a46b486cd1f8d92b06cab");'><span id='0e23f6c6287a46b486cd1f8d92b06cab_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>，50岁</div><div id='0e23f6c6287a46b486cd1f8d92b06cab' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>贾似道疑廷鸾托疾，自出关访之，实觇之，见其骨立，始信其真病。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作诗咏树，以寄其志。作品：《带湖春树先和公手植也感而有赋》<div id='poem_56647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_56647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/56647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>带湖春树先和公手植也感而有赋<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1271年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(35528, "宋末元初", "马廷鸾", id='poem_sentence_0_56647'>暗香疏影久凄迷，咫尺塘边丈尺泥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56647'>培植莫教阳德尽，看花踏雪过前堤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56646'>老树今踰七十霜，冰魂玉骨自孤芳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_56646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_56646'>大家扶起摧残后，此是吾家召伯棠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_56646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_56646'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_56646_comment'></div></div><div
